###begin article-title 0
###xml 17 39 17 39 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Caenorhabditis elegans</italic>
###xml 102 109 102 109 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">In Vivo</italic>
###xml 17 39 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">Caenorhabditis elegans</span>
Mutations in the Caenorhabditis elegans U2AF Large Subunit UAF-1 Alter the Choice of a 3' Splice Site In Vivo
###end article-title 0
###begin p 1
Conceived and designed the experiments: LM HRH. Performed the experiments: LM. Analyzed the data: LM HRH. Wrote the paper: LM HRH.
###end p 1
###begin p 2
###xml 273 280 273 280 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 342 378 342 378 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Caenorhabditis elegans unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 454 464 454 464 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 556 568 556 568 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 637 643 637 643 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 721 734 721 734 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 758 770 758 770 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 859 871 859 871 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 926 931 926 931 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1241 1247 1235 1241 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1563 1576 1557 1570 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1594 1606 1588 1600 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1611 1623 1605 1617 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 1707 1714 1701 1708 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 1838 1845 1832 1839 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 1876 1886 1870 1880 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 342 364 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">Caenorhabditis elegans</span>
###xml 454 464 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 1876 1886 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
The removal of introns from eukaryotic RNA transcripts requires the activities of five multi-component ribonucleoprotein complexes and numerous associated proteins. The lack of mutations affecting splicing factors essential for animal survival has limited the study of the in vivo regulation of splicing. From a screen for suppressors of the Caenorhabditis elegans unc-93(e1500) rubberband Unc phenotype, we identified mutations in genes that encode the C. elegans orthologs of two splicing factors, the U2AF large subunit (UAF-1) and SF1/BBP (SFA-1). The uaf-1(n4588) mutation resulted in temperature-sensitive lethality and caused the unc-93 RNA transcript to be spliced using a cryptic 3' splice site generated by the unc-93(e1500) missense mutation. The sfa-1(n4562) mutation did not cause the utilization of this cryptic 3' splice site. We isolated four uaf-1(n4588) intragenic suppressors that restored the viability of uaf-1 mutants at 25degreesC. These suppressors differentially affected the recognition of the cryptic 3' splice site and implicated a small region of UAF-1 between the U2AF small subunit-interaction domain and the first RNA recognition motif in affecting the choice of 3' splice site. We constructed a reporter for unc-93 splicing and using site-directed mutagenesis found that the position of the cryptic splice site affects its recognition. We also identified nucleotides of the endogenous 3' splice site important for recognition by wild-type UAF-1. Our genetic and molecular analyses suggested that the phenotypic suppression of the unc-93(e1500) Unc phenotype by uaf-1(n4588) and sfa-1(n4562) was likely caused by altered splicing of an unknown gene. Our observations provide in vivo evidence that UAF-1 can act in regulating 3' splice-site choice and establish a system that can be used to investigate the in vivo regulation of RNA splicing in C. elegans.
###end p 2
###begin title 3
Author Summary
###end title 3
###begin p 4
###xml 266 288 266 288 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Caenorhabditis elegans</italic>
###xml 459 465 459 465 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 578 584 578 584 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 605 612 605 612 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 965 972 965 972 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 1184 1191 1184 1191 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 266 288 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">Caenorhabditis elegans</span>
Eukaryotic genes contain intervening intronic sequences that must be removed from pre-mRNA transcripts by RNA splicing to generate functional messenger RNAs. While studying genes that encode and control a presumptive muscle potassium channel complex in the nematode Caenorhabditis elegans, we found that mutations in two splicing factors, the U2AF large subunit and SF1/BBP suppress the rubberband Unc phenotype caused by a rare missense mutation in the gene unc-93. Mutations affecting the U2AF large subunit caused the recognition of a cryptic 3' splice site generated by the unc-93 mutation, providing in vivo evidence that the U2AF large subunit can affect splice-site selection. By contrast, an SF1/BBP mutation that suppressed the rubberband Unc phenotype did not cause splicing using this cryptic 3' splice site. Our genetic studies identified a region of the U2AF large subunit important for its effect on 3' splice-site choice. Our mutagenesis analysis of in vivo transgene splicing identified a positional effect on weak 3' splice site selection and nucleotides of the endogenous 3' splice site important for recognition. The system we have defined should facilitate future in vivo analyses of pre-mRNA splicing.
###end p 4

Introduction
###end title 5
###begin p 6
###xml 125 128 125 128 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Maniatis1">[1]</xref>
###xml 129 132 129 132 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Reed1">[2]</xref>
###xml 329 332 329 332 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Maniatis1">[1]</xref>
###xml 333 336 333 336 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Graveley1">[3]</xref>
###xml 337 340 337 340 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Smith1">[4]</xref>
###xml 345 355 345 355 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 435 438 435 438 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zahler1">[5]</xref>
###xml 488 491 488 491 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Johnson1">[6]</xref>
###xml 492 495 492 495 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Wang1">[7]</xref>
###xml 559 569 559 569 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Drosophila</italic>
###xml 575 580 575 580 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dscam</italic>
###xml 582 583 582 583 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">D</underline>
###xml 587 588 587 588 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</underline>
###xml 596 597 596 597 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">c</underline>
###xml 601 602 601 602 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</underline>
###xml 610 611 610 611 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">m</underline>
###xml 704 707 704 707 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Schmucker1">[8]</xref>
###xml 783 786 783 786 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Watson1">[9]</xref>
###xml 813 817 813 817 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Hughes1">[10]</xref>
###xml 818 822 818 822 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Wojtowicz1">[12]</xref>
###xml 917 921 917 921 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Cartegni1">[13]</xref>
###xml 922 926 922 926 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Wang2">[14]</xref>
###xml 345 355 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 443 449 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">humans</span>
###xml 902 907 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">human</span>
Eukaryotic genes contain intervening introns that are spliced from transcribed pre-mRNAs to generate functional coding mRNAs [1],[2]. Alternative splicing results in distinct mRNAs that encode proteins with distinct functions, increases the proteome size and is believed to be important to the biological complexity of metazoans [1],[3],[4]. In C. elegans, mRNA transcripts of at least 13% of predicted genes are alternatively spliced [5]. In humans, most genes are alternatively spliced [6],[7]. A dramatic example of alternative splicing is provided by the Drosophila gene Dscam (Down syndrome cell adhesion molecule), which through alternative splicing could potentially generate over 30,000 isoforms [8], some of which have been shown to play important roles in immune responses [9] and neuronal arborization [10]-[12]. Mutations affecting the splicing process or splicing machinery cause numerous human diseases [13],[14].
###end p 6
###begin p 7
###xml 115 118 115 118 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Maniatis1">[1]</xref>
###xml 119 122 119 122 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Reed1">[2]</xref>
###xml 123 127 123 127 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Guthrie1">[15]</xref>
###xml 264 268 264 268 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Madhani1">[16]</xref>
###xml 341 342 341 342 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</underline>
###xml 350 351 350 351 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">f</underline>
###xml 361 362 361 362 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">b</underline>
###xml 374 375 374 375 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">b</underline>
###xml 382 383 382 383 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">p</underline>
###xml 433 437 433 437 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">U2 a</underline>
###xml 446 447 446 447 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">f</underline>
###xml 454 458 454 458 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Abovich1">[17]</xref>
###xml 459 463 459 463 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio1">[23]</xref>
###xml 647 651 647 651 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Krainer1">[19]</xref>
###xml 653 657 653 657 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Wu1">[21]</xref>
###xml 659 663 659 663 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Berglund1">[24]</xref>
###xml 664 668 664 668 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zamore3">[26]</xref>
###xml 680 704 680 704 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Saccharomyces cerevisiae</italic>
###xml 906 910 906 910 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Abovich1">[17]</xref>
###xml 911 915 911 915 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Berglund1">[24]</xref>
###xml 916 920 916 920 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Abovich2">[27]</xref>
###xml 921 925 921 925 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Berglund2">[28]</xref>
###xml 943 965 943 965 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Caenorhabditis elegans</italic>
###xml 1217 1221 1217 1221 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio1">[23]</xref>
###xml 1222 1226 1222 1226 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Hollins1">[29]</xref>
###xml 674 679 <span type="species:ncbi:4932">yeast</span>
###xml 680 704 <span type="species:ncbi:4932">Saccharomyces cerevisiae</span>
###xml 943 965 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">Caenorhabditis elegans</span>
Pre-mRNA splicing involves five small nuclear ribonucleoprotein particles (snRNPs) and numerous associated factors [1],[2],[15]. The U1 snRNP recognizes the 5' splice donor site through base-pairing between the U1 snRNA and the 5' splice site of the target intron [16]. The recognition of the 3' splice acceptor site is achieved by SF1/BBP (splicing factor one/branch-point binding protein) and the large and small subunits of U2AF (U2 auxiliary factor) [17]-[23]. In mammals, SF1/BBP binds a weak consensus branch-point sequence, the U2AF large subunit binds a long polypyrimidine sequence and the U2AF small subunit binds the 3' splice site YAG [19], [21], [24]-[26]. The yeast Saccharomyces cerevisiae lacks a U2AF small subunit and a polypyrimidine sequence in its introns, and the recognition of a 3' splice site is achieved by binding of SF1/BBP to a highly conserved consensus branch-point sequence [17],[24],[27],[28]. In the nematode Caenorhabditis elegans, there is no consensus branch-point sequence or long polypyrimidine sequence, and the recognition of a 3' splice site is achieved by the binding of the U2AF large and small subunits to a consensus UUUUCAGR sequence in which "AG" is the 3' splice site [23],[29].
###end p 7
###begin p 8
###xml 36 37 36 37 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">r</underline>
###xml 44 45 44 45 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">S</underline>
###xml 80 84 80 84 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Fu1">[30]</xref>
###xml 85 89 85 89 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zahler2">[33]</xref>
###xml 121 124 121 124 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Smith1">[4]</xref>
###xml 266 269 266 269 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Smith1">[4]</xref>
Splicing is also regulated by many Arginine-Serine-rich RNA-binding SR proteins [30]-[33] and hnRNP RNA-binding proteins [4]. These splicing factors recognize enhancer or silencer sequences in exons and introns to regulate the specificity and efficiency of splicing [4]. The genetic interactions among splicing factors and how signaling events regulate splicing efficiency and specificity are only partially understood.
###end p 8
###begin p 9
###xml 0 10 0 10 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 158 164 158 164 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 166 171 166 171 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 176 182 176 182 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 224 234 224 234 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 252 253 252 253 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+</sup>
###xml 299 303 299 303 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-delaCruz1">[34]</xref>
###xml 304 308 304 308 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin1">[37]</xref>
###xml 315 316 315 316 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">g</underline>
###xml 323 324 323 324 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">f</underline>
###xml 453 454 453 454 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+</sup>
###xml 676 677 676 677 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">l</underline>
###xml 684 685 684 685 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">f</underline>
###xml 711 717 711 717 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 719 724 719 724 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 729 735 729 735 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 775 779 775 779 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald1">[35]</xref>
###xml 780 784 780 784 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald2">[36]</xref>
###xml 832 833 832 833 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">T</underline>
###xml 841 842 841 842 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">A</underline>
###xml 846 847 846 847 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">S</underline>
###xml 856 857 856 857 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">K</underline>
###xml 857 858 857 858 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+</sup>
###xml 886 890 886 890 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-delaCruz1">[34]</xref>
###xml 892 898 892 898 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 989 993 989 993 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-delaCruz1">[34]</xref>
###xml 995 1001 995 1001 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1105 1115 1105 1115 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 1127 1131 1127 1131 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-delaCruz1">[34]</xref>
###xml 1132 1136 1132 1136 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin1">[37]</xref>
###xml 1296 1300 1296 1300 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Brinkmann1">[38]</xref>
###xml 1301 1305 1301 1305 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Tabeta1">[42]</xref>
###xml 0 10 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 224 234 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 1105 1115 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
C. elegans is a genetically tractable organism and has been used to study a broad variety of biological problems. Our laboratory has analyzed a set of genes, unc-93, sup-9 and sup-10, that encode components of a presumptive C. elegans two-pore domain K+ channel complex and regulate muscle activity [34]-[37]. Rare gain-of-function (gf) mutations in any of these three genes cause abnormal body-muscle contraction and are thought to activate the SUP-9 K+ channel. The gf mutant animals are defective in egg laying, sluggish and exhibit a rubberband phenotype: when prodded on the head, the animal contracts and relaxes along its entire body without moving backwards. Complete loss-of-function (lf) mutations of unc-93, sup-9 and sup-10 do not cause any obvious abnormalities [35],[36]. The SUP-9 protein is similar to the mammalian Two-pore Acid Sensitive K+ channels TASK-1 and TASK-3 [34]. sup-10 encodes a novel single-transmembrane domain protein without identified mammalian homologs [34]. unc-93 encodes a multiple transmembrane-domain protein that defines a novel family of proteins conserved from C. elegans to mammals [34],[37]. A mammalian UNC-93 homolog, UNC-93b, plays important roles in the innate immune response, probably by regulating signals mediated through Toll-like receptors [38]-[42].
###end p 9
###begin p 10
###xml 65 71 65 71 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 73 78 73 78 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 83 89 83 89 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 298 304 298 304 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 317 322 317 322 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">e1500</italic>
###xml 457 464 457 464 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 493 503 493 503 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 493 503 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
Previous genetic screens for genes that affect the activities of unc-93, sup-9 and sup-10 genes were not designed to identify genes essential for fertility or animal survival. To seek such essential genes, we performed a clonal genetic screen for suppressors of the locomotion defect caused by the unc-93 gf mutation e1500. In this paper, we describe our studies of two suppressors identified from this screen and the establishment of a reporter system for in vivo analysis of RNA splicing in C. elegans. We suggest that the U2AF large subunit affects 3' splice site recognition and that some aspect of the function of the putative UNC-93/SUP-9/SUP-10 two-pore domain potassium channel complex depends on an unidentified gene the processing of which requires the functions of the U2AF large subunit and SF1/BBP.
###end p 10
###begin title 11
Results
###end title 11
###begin title 12
###xml 35 48 35 48 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
A clonal screen identified two new unc-93(e1500) suppressor genes essential for suvival
###end title 12
###begin p 13
###xml 25 35 25 35 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 42 48 42 48 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 50 55 50 55 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 60 66 60 66 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 182 186 182 186 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald1">[35]</xref>
###xml 187 191 187 191 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald2">[36]</xref>
###xml 192 196 192 196 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin2">[43]</xref>
###xml 329 333 329 333 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald1">[35]</xref>
###xml 334 338 334 338 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald2">[36]</xref>
###xml 339 343 339 343 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin2">[43]</xref>
###xml 344 348 344 348 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-DeStasio1">[44]</xref>
###xml 457 470 457 470 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 564 585 564 585 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 614 615 614 615 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">1</sub>
###xml 671 672 671 672 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">0</sub>
###xml 703 704 703 704 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">e</underline>
###xml 709 710 709 710 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">m</underline>
###xml 716 717 716 717 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</underline>
###xml 756 761 756 761 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 766 771 766 771 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 773 778 773 778 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 825 830 819 824 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 911 916 905 910 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 921 926 915 920 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 1024 1045 1018 1039 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 25 35 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
Rare gf mutations in the C. elegans genes unc-93, sup-9 and sup-10 cause a rubberband Unc phenotype, while lf mutations in these genes result in a phenotypically wild-type phenotype [35],[36],[43]. Previous screens for suppressors of the rubberband Unc phenotype were not designed to identify genes essential for animal survival [35],[36],[43],[44]. We performed a clonal genetic screen to seek new suppressors of the rubberband Unc phenotype caused by the unc-93(e1500) mutation, with the goal of identifying mutations that also cause sterility or lethality (see Materials and Methods). We screened about 10,000 F1 progeny (about 20,000 mutagenized haploid genomes) of P0 animals mutagenized with EMS (ethyl methanesulfonate) and isolated the suppressors n4588 and n4562. n4588 causes embryonic lethality at 25degreesC, and n4562 causes sterility at all temperatures. By mapping these mutations, we found that n4588 and n4562 are not alleles of any previously characterized suppressors of the rubberband Unc phenotype (see Materials and Methods).
###end p 13
###begin title 14
###xml 0 5 0 5 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 32 37 32 37 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 57 67 57 67 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 57 67 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
n4588 is a missense mutation in uaf-1, which encodes the C. elegans ortholog of the U2AF large subunit splicing factor
###end title 14
###begin p 15
###xml 0 5 0 5 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>

###xml 125 130 125 130 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>

###xml 291 312 285 306 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>

###xml 499 504 481 486 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 563 584 545 566 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 779 784 761 766 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 786 792 768 774 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 796 805 778 787 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1A</xref>
###xml 916 922 898 904 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 935 945 917 927 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 1005 1007 987 989 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">U2</underline>
###xml 1007 1008 989 990 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</underline>
###xml 1017 1018 999 1000 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">f</underline>
###xml 1025 1029 1007 1011 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio2">[45]</xref>
###xml 1127 1131 1109 1113 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zamore2">[25]</xref>
###xml 1132 1136 1114 1118 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Ruskin1">[46]</xref>
###xml 1171 1181 1153 1163 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 1265 1267 1247 1249 <bold xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">AG</bold>
###xml 1313 1317 1295 1299 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio1">[23]</xref>
###xml 1318 1322 1300 1304 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Hollins1">[29]</xref>
###xml 1393 1402 1375 1384 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1B</xref>
###xml 1450 1459 1432 1441 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1B</xref>
###xml 1474 1475 1456 1457 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">R</underline>
###xml 1478 1479 1460 1461 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">r</underline>
###xml 1490 1491 1472 1473 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">m</underline>
###xml 1506 1515 1488 1497 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1B</xref>
###xml 1522 1526 1504 1508 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zamore3">[26]</xref>
###xml 1527 1531 1509 1513 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Rudner1">[47]</xref>
###xml 1554 1555 1536 1537 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">U</underline>
###xml 1559 1560 1541 1542 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">h</underline>
###xml 1568 1569 1550 1551 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">m</underline>
###xml 1621 1625 1603 1607 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Selenko1">[48]</xref>
###xml 1658 1663 1640 1645 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 1764 1773 1746 1755 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1B</xref>
###xml 935 945 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 1171 1181 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
n4588 is a strong recessive suppressor of the locomotion defect and rubberband phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals (Table 1). n4588 is or is closely linked to a mutation that causes a recessive temperature-sensitive (ts) lethal phenotype and results in embryonic lethality at 25degreesC (see Materials and Methods) (data not shown). At 20degreesC the lethal phenotype was incompletely penetrant. At 15degreesC n4588 animals appeared similar to wild-type animals. We mapped the ts-lethal phenotype of n4588 animals to an 80 kb region on the left arm of LG III (see Materials and Methods). By determining the sequences of the coding exons of four of eight genes located within this 80 kb interval, we found a point mutation in the third coding exon of the major isoform of the gene uaf-1 (uaf-1a in Figure 1A), changing codon 180 from ACT to ATT, a change predicted to replace a conserved threonine with an isoleucine. uaf-1a encodes the C. elegans ortholog of the highly conserved U2AF large subunit (U2AF, U2auxiliary factor) [45]. In mammals, the U2AF large subunit binds a polypyrimidine sequence preceding the 3' splice site [25],[46] to regulate pre-mRNA splicing. In C. elegans, together with the U2AF small subunit ortholog UAF-2, UAF-1 binds a consensus UUUUCAGR sequence, in which AG is the 3' splice site [23],[29]. The U2AF large subunit contains an RS-rich (Arginine-Serine) domain (Figure 1B, RS), a U2AF small subunit-interacting domain (Figure 1B, W), two RRM (RNA recognition motif) domains (Figure 1B, RRM) [26],[47] and a C-terminal UHM (U2AF homology motif) domain that binds the splicing factor SF1/BBP [48]. The T180I change caused by the n4588 mutation lies between the U2AF small subunit-interacting domain and the first RRM domain of UAF-1a (Figure 1B).
###end p 15
###begin title 16
###xml 0 5 0 5 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
uaf-1 gene and proteins.
###end title 16
###begin p 17
###xml 29 34 29 34 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 44 50 44 50 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 55 61 55 61 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1b</italic>
###xml 92 96 92 96 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio2">[45]</xref>
###xml 119 124 119 124 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 151 156 151 156 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 343 349 343 349 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 361 365 361 365 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio2">[45]</xref>
###xml 414 420 414 420 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 425 431 425 431 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1b</italic>

###begin p 22
###xml 48 54 48 54 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 97 102 97 102 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 199 204 199 204 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">myo-3</italic>
###xml 282 286 282 286 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Okkema1">[49]</xref>
###xml 293 299 293 299 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 404 430 404 430 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 440 449 440 449 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1B</xref>
###xml 454 461 454 461 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t002">Table 2</xref>
###xml 482 487 482 487 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 497 503 497 503 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1b</italic>
###xml 623 632 623 632 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1B</xref>
###xml 637 644 637 644 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t002">Table 2</xref>
###xml 667 672 667 672 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">myo-3</italic>
###xml 692 698 692 698 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 703 709 703 709 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1b</italic>
###xml 855 860 855 860 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 897 903 897 903 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 942 949 942 949 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t002">Table 2</xref>
###xml 1023 1029 1023 1029 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 1074 1078 1074 1078 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Stringham1">[50]</xref>
###xml 1121 1134 1121 1134 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1138 1150 1138 1150 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1182 1194 1182 1194 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1196 1203 1196 1203 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t002">Table 2</xref>
###xml 1305 1318 1305 1318 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1332 1337 1332 1337 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1364 1373 1364 1373 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1B</xref>
###xml 1378 1399 1378 1399 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 1446 1453 1446 1453 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t002">Table 2</xref>
###xml 1493 1498 1493 1498 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1554 1567 1554 1567 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
To test whether the point mutation found in the uaf-1a isoform caused the suppressor activity of n4588, we generated transgenic animals expressing a UAF-1a::GFP fusion protein under the control of a myo-3 myosin promoter, which drives transgene expression in body-wall muscle cells [49]. This uaf-1a cDNA, which encodes a predicted full-length UAF-1 protein, restored the Unc phenotype when expressed in uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500) animals (Figure 1B and Table 2). A predicted short uaf-1 isoform, uaf-1b, which contains only part of the second RRM domain and the C-terminal UHM domain, failed to restore the Unc phenotype (Figure 1B and Table 2). Expression of these myo-3-driven transgenes (uaf-1a and uaf-1b) in wild-type animals did not cause a rubberband Unc phenotype or any other visible abnormality (data not shown). Introducing stop codons or the n4588 T180I mutation into the full-length uaf-1a cDNA abrogated its rescuing activity (Table 2). Heat-shock-driven expression of a transgene expressing the full-length uaf-1a cDNA under control of a heat-shock promoter [50] partially rescued both the suppression of unc-93(e1500) by uaf-1(n4588) and the ts-lethality caused by uaf-1(n4588) (Table 2 and data not shown), suggesting that the T180I mutation also caused the ts-lethal phenotype. Feeding unc-93(e1500) animals with uaf-1 RNAi-expressing bacteria (Figure 1B and Materials and Methods) also partially suppressed the Unc phenotype (Table 2), suggesting that normal expression of uaf-1 is required for the rubberband Unc phenotype caused by unc-93(e1500).
###end p 22

uaf-1a and sfa-1 transgenes rescued the suppression of the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals by uaf-1(n4588) and sfa-1(n4562).

###xml 537 550 537 550 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>

###begin p 25
###xml 14 19 14 19 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 39 44 39 44 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 158 164 154 160 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 174 183 170 179 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1A</xref>
###xml 281 287 277 283 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 318 323 314 319 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 324 329 320 325 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 385 390 377 382 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 391 396 383 388 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 454 467 442 455 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 494 499 482 487 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 500 505 488 493 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 674 679 658 663 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 709 730 689 710 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 733 751 713 731 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)/uaf-1</italic>
###xml 752 757 732 737 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 807 820 783 796 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 859 871 835 847 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 873 880 849 856 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t001">Table 1</xref>
###xml 894 906 870 882 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 920 938 896 914 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)/uaf-1</italic>
###xml 939 944 915 920 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 1039 1044 1005 1010 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 1061 1066 1027 1032 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1103 1115 1069 1081 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1197 1210 1163 1176 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1244 1256 1210 1222 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1291 1296 1257 1262 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1320 1325 1286 1291 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1372 1377 1338 1343 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1388 1398 1354 1364 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s3">Discussion</xref>
We isolated a uaf-1 deletion mutation, n5222Delta, which removes the fourth exon (encoding part of the first RRM and part of the second RRM of UAF-1a) of the uaf-1a isoform (Figure 1A) and is predicted to cause a frameshift after amino acid 229 if the third and fifth exons of the uaf-1a isoform are spliced together. uaf-1(n5222Delta)/+ animals grew and moved like the wild type, and uaf-1(n5222Delta)/+ did not suppress the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals (data not shown). uaf-1(n5222Delta) homozygous mutants arrested and died at the late L1 to early L2 larval stages (based on body size), which precluded examination of the rubberband Unc behavior of n5222Delta homozygous animals (see Materials and Methods). uaf-1(n4588)/uaf-1(n5222Delta) suppressed the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals as strongly as did homozygous uaf-1(n4588) (Table 1). Similar to uaf-1(n4588) homozygotes, uaf-1(n4588)/uaf-1(n5222Delta) animals died embryonically at 25degreesC (data not shown). These results establish that n4588 is an allele of uaf-1 and that reducing the dosage of the uaf-1(n4588) allele by 50% does not affect the suppression of the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals. These data suggest that uaf-1(n4588) causes either a reduction/loss of uaf-1 activity or an altered uaf-1 activity that is antagonized by the wild-type uaf-1 gene (see Discussion).
###end p 25
###begin title 26
###xml 0 12 0 12 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
uaf-1(n4588) differentially suppressed different rubberband Unc mutants
###end title 26
###begin p 27
###xml 46 59 46 59 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 83 95 83 95 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(n200)</italic>
###xml 105 109 105 109 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald2">[36]</xref>
###xml 143 148 143 148 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 153 159 153 159 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 159 163 159 163 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald1">[35]</xref>
###xml 164 168 164 168 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin2">[43]</xref>
###xml 192 204 192 204 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 280 287 280 287 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t001">Table 1</xref>
###xml 370 382 370 382 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(n200)</italic>
###xml 401 413 401 413 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 415 422 415 422 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t001">Table 1</xref>
###xml 425 437 425 437 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
###xml 512 524 512 524 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(n200)</italic>
###xml 562 575 562 575 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 614 626 614 626 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 628 635 628 635 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t001">Table 1</xref>
###xml 671 683 671 683 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9(n1550)</italic>
###xml 683 687 683 687 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin2">[43]</xref>
###xml 711 723 711 723 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 725 732 725 732 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t001">Table 1</xref>
###xml 759 771 759 771 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 808 814 808 814 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 955 961 955 961 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 963 968 963 968 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 973 979 973 979 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 985 995 985 995 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s3">Discussion</xref>
Locomotion defects similar to those caused by unc-93(e1500) are also caused by the unc-93(n200) mutation [36] and by gf mutations in the genes sup-9 and sup-10[35],[43]. We tested whether the uaf-1(n4588) mutation could suppress the Unc phenotype caused by these other mutations (Table 1). Neither the weak locomotion defect nor the weak rubberband Unc defect caused by unc-93(n200) was suppressed by uaf-1(n4588) (Table 1). sup-10(n983), which causes a rubberband Unc phenotype that is more severe than that of unc-93(n200) animals but less severe than that of unc-93(e1500) animals, was completely suppressed by uaf-1(n4588) (Table 1). The strongest rubberband mutant, sup-9(n1550)[43], was not suppressed by uaf-1(n4588) (Table 1). These data suggest that uaf-1(n4588) is an allele-specific suppressor of unc-93 but not a gene-specific suppressor of the rubberband Unc mutants and is distinct in its suppression pattern from other known suppressors of unc-93, sup-9 and sup-10 (see Discussion).
###end p 27
###begin p 28
###xml 18 24 18 24 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 26 32 26 32 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 37 42 37 42 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 104 108 104 108 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald1">[35]</xref>
###xml 109 113 109 113 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald2">[36]</xref>
###xml 177 182 177 182 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 224 236 224 236 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 259 265 259 265 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 267 273 267 273 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 277 282 277 282 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 365 377 365 377 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 401 409 401 409 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s005">Table S1</xref>
###xml 428 434 428 434 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 436 442 436 442 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 447 452 447 452 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 489 494 489 494 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 515 527 515 527 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 656 668 656 668 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 686 700 686 700 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-58(e665sd)</italic>
###xml 700 704 700 704 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Park1">[51]</xref>
###xml 742 756 742 756 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">egl-23(n601sd)</italic>
###xml 756 760 756 760 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Trent1">[52]</xref>
###xml 800 815 800 815 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">twk-18(e1913sd)</italic>
###xml 815 819 815 819 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Kunkel1">[53]</xref>
###xml 894 906 894 906 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 908 916 908 916 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s005">Table S1</xref>
Null mutations of unc-93, sup-10 and sup-9 do not cause visible abnormalities in a wild-type background [35],[36]. We tested whether these genes might function redundantly with uaf-1, by generating double mutants containing uaf-1(n4588) and null mutations of unc-93, sup-10 or sup-9. We found that such double mutant animals grew and behaved indistinguishably from uaf-1(n4588) single mutant animals (Table S1), suggesting that unc-93, sup-10 and sup-9 are not functionally redundant with uaf-1. To examine whether uaf-1(n4588) can suppress gf mutations affecting other two-pore domain potassium channels, we generated double mutant animals containing the uaf-1(n4588) mutation and the unc-58(e665sd)[51] (J. Thomas, personal communication), egl-23(n601sd)[52] (J. Thomas, personal communication) or twk-18(e1913sd)[53] mutations. The behavioral defects of these mutants were not suppressed by uaf-1(n4588) (Table S1).
###end p 28
###begin p 29
###xml 34 40 34 40 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 42 47 42 47 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>

###xml 131 143 131 143 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 165 171 165 171 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 173 179 173 179 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 181 186 181 186 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 188 194 188 194 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-18</italic>
###xml 194 198 194 198 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald1">[35]</xref>
###xml 257 263 257 263 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-11</italic>
###xml 263 267 263 267 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald3">[54]</xref>
###xml 355 361 355 361 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 363 369 363 369 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 374 379 374 379 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 397 403 397 403 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-18</italic>
###xml 424 430 424 430 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-11</italic>
###xml 499 505 499 505 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 507 512 507 512 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 517 523 517 523 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 620 629 620 629 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s001">Figure S1</xref>
###xml 704 708 704 708 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio2">[45]</xref>
###xml 788 800 788 800 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 862 875 862 875 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 879 891 879 891 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
To determine if the expression of unc-93, sup-9, sup-10 or any of the other genes known to interact with these genes is reduced in uaf-1(n4588) animals, we examined unc-93, sup-10, sup-9, sup-18[35] (I. Perez de la Cruz and H.R.H., unpublished results) and sup-11[54] (E. Alvarez-Saavedra and H.R.H, unpublished results) mRNA levels. Like lf mutations in unc-93, sup-10 and sup-9, lf mutations in sup-18 and gf mutations in sup-11 can suppress the rubberband Unc phenotype caused by gf mutations in unc-93, sup-9 and sup-10. Using real-time qRT-PCR, we found no obvious reduction of the mRNA levels of these five genes (Figure S1). We also examined the expression of UAF-1 protein using western blotting [45] and found no apparent difference in UAF-1 protein levels between wild-type and uaf-1(n4588) animals (data not shown), suggesting that the suppression of unc-93(e1500) by uaf-1(n4588) is not caused by a reduction of the level of the UAF-1 protein.
###end p 29
###begin title 30
###xml 0 12 0 12 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 37 50 37 50 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 115 128 115 128 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
uaf-1(n4588) altered the splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 by recognizing a cryptic 3' splice site generated by the unc-93(e1500) missense mutation

###xml 1525 1529 1525 1529 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin1">[37]</xref>
###xml 1531 1540 1531 1540 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g002">Figure 2E</xref>
###xml 1583 1592 1583 1592 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4A</xref>
###xml 1690 1696 1690 1696 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1707 1720 1707 1720 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1740 1766 1740 1766 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1776 1785 1776 1785 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4B</xref>
###xml 1811 1820 1811 1820 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g002">Figure 2C</xref>
###xml 1847 1856 1847 1856 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4B</xref>
###xml 1929 1941 1929 1941 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1943 1955 1943 1955 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(n200)</italic>
###xml 1959 1984 1959 1984 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(n200)</italic>
###xml 2053 2066 2053 2066 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
We tested whether the splicing of unc-93 is altered by uaf-1(n4588). We examined the splicing of each exon of unc-93 in wild-type, uaf-1(n4588), unc-93(e1500), uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500), unc-93(n200) and uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(n200) animals by RT-PCR (Figure 2). Every exon other than exon 9 of the unc-93 gene was spliced similarly in all genotypes examined (Figure 2A and 2B). However, we had difficulty in consistently amplifying a cDNA band from uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500) animals (data not shown) using the PCR primer pairs at the 3' end of exon 8 and the 5' end of exon 9 (indicated in black in Figure 2A). We therefore used a new pair of PCR primers that should amplify a larger region between exons 8 and 9 (Figure 2A, red arrows). With the new pair of PCR primers, we found that in unc-93(e1500) animals the region between exon 8 and 9 corresponded to a weak but consistent RT-PCR product of a reduced length (Figure 2C, lane 3, lower arrow), and this RT-PCR product was seen only in samples from unc-93(e1500) mutant animals (Figure 2C, lower arrow). In uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500) animals, the RT-PCR product of reduced length was the most prominent product (Figure 2C, lane 4, lower arrow). We determined the sequence of this RT-PCR product and found that it was a consequence of an alternative splicing event that utilized a cryptic 3' splice site in exon 9. This cryptic 3' splice site was generated by the unc-93(e1500) missense mutation, which has a G-to-A transition that changes amino acid 388 from Gly to Arg [37] (Figure 2E). Quantification using Taqman RT-PCR (see Figure 4A for probe designs) indicated that the alternatively spliced exon 9 was about 1.3% of all spliced unc-93 exon 9 in unc-93(e1500) animals and 68% in uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500) animals (Figure 4B). Both non-quantitative (Figure 2C) and quantitative RT-PCR (Figure 4B) analyses failed to detect alternatively spliced exon 9 from wild-type, uaf-1(n4588), unc-93(n200) or uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(n200) animals, all of which lack the cryptic 3' splice site caused by the unc-93(e1500) mutation.
###end p 31
###begin title 32
###xml 0 12 0 12 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 33 46 33 46 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 55 64 55 64 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(+)</italic>
uaf-1(n4588) dramatically alters unc-93(e1500) but not unc-93(+) exon 9 splicing.
###end title 32

###xml 29 35 29 35 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 51 57 51 57 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 177 203 177 203 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 419 432 419 432 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 491 497 491 497 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 764 770 764 770 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 794 807 794 807 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 842 868 842 868 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1117 1123 1117 1123 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1208 1221 1208 1221 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1447 1460 1447 1460 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1502 1508 1502 1508 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1601 1614 1601 1614 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1668 1673 1668 1673 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">e1500</italic>
###xml 1812 1824 1812 1824 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
(A) Genomic structure of the unc-93 gene. Exons of unc-93 are indicated by black boxes and introns by thin lines. The part of exon 9 that was removed by alternative splicing in uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500) animals is marked as a red box. Exonic primers (arrows) flanking each intron were used to amplify mRNA regions of each exon-exon junction. The red primer pair was used to identify the alternative splice products of unc-93(e1500) exon 9. (B) RT-PCR experiments to examine the splicing of unc-93 mRNA. En-En+1 (arrows) indicates the junction of two adjacent exons. Genotypes of each sample are indicated at the top. Small arrowheads indicate primer dimers, which form variably in RT-PCR experiments and are template-independent. (C) A weak alternatively spliced unc-93 exon 9 was detected in unc-93(e1500) animals (lane 3, lower arrow). In uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500) animals (lane 4, lower arrow), this alternative spliced product was dramatically enhanced. The diagrams on the left illustrate the splicing events responsible for the generation of each band. The upper band reflects the splicing seen for wild-type unc-93, while the lower band reflects the use of a cryptic 3' splice site generated by the unc-93(e1500) missense mutation. Red arrows indicate the positions of PCR primers. Genotypes of each sample are listed at the top. (D) Reducing UAF-1 levels with RNAi did not cause increased splicing at the cryptic 3' splice site found in unc-93(e1500) exon 9. (E) Partial genomic sequences of unc-93 intron 8 (lowercase letters) and exon 9 (uppercase letters) in the wild type (above) and in unc-93(e1500) mutants (below). The G-to-A nucleotide change of the e1500 mutation is indicated with an arrow. The AG sequence (red) forms a cryptic 3' splice site that is recognized by the splicing machinery in uaf-1(n4588) animals.
