###xml 26 32 26 32 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 156 160 156 160 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin1">[37]</xref>
###xml 221 227 221 227 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 242 268 242 268 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 364 376 364 376 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9(n1550)</italic>
###xml 378 384 378 384 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 385 389 385 389 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">lr12</italic>
###xml 404 408 400 404 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-delaCruz1">[34]</xref>
###xml 409 413 405 409 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-DeStasio1">[44]</xref>
###xml 490 498 486 494 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s006">Table S2</xref>
###xml 542 548 538 544 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 672 678 668 674 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 818 824 814 820 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 869 875 865 871 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 909 922 905 918 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 932 940 928 936 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s007">Table S3</xref>
###xml 986 1001 982 997 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)/+</italic>
###xml 1038 1051 1034 1047 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1060 1064 1056 1060 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald2">[36]</xref>
###xml 1065 1069 1061 1065 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin1">[37]</xref>
###xml 1099 1105 1095 1101 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1151 1164 1147 1160 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1174 1182 1170 1178 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s007">Table S3</xref>
###xml 1214 1220 1210 1216 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1376 1388 1372 1384 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1416 1422 1412 1418 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1492 1505 1488 1501 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1564 1570 1560 1566 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1645 1658 1641 1654 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1668 1676 1664 1672 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s007">Table S3</xref>
###xml 1721 1727 1717 1723 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1756 1762 1752 1758 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1810 1816 1806 1812 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
The alternatively spliced unc-93 transcript is predicted to encode a truncated protein lacking 12 amino acids in one of the predicted transmembrane domains [37] (data not shown). To test whether the alternatively spliced unc-93 transcript in uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500) animals encoded a functional UNC-93 protein, we expressed the cDNA in the body-wall muscles of sup-9(n1550); unc-93(lr12Delta) animals [34],[44] and found that this transgene did not restore the rubberband Unc phenotype (Table S2). By contrast, expression of the wild-type unc-93 cDNA in these animals restored the severe rubberband Unc phenotype. These results suggested that the alternatively spliced unc-93 transcript encoded a lf UNC-93 protein or possibly a dominant-negative UNC-93 protein. To test the latter possibility, we expressed either unc-93 wild-type cDNA or the alternatively spliced unc-93 cDNA in the body-wall muscles of unc-93(e1500) animals (Table S3). Consistent with previous observations that unc-93(e1500)/+ animals have better locomotion than unc-93(e1500) animals [36],[37], overexpression of wild-type unc-93 cDNA dramatically improved the locomotion of unc-93(e1500) animals (Table S3). If the alternatively spliced unc-93 transcript encoded an UNC-93 protein that could interfere with the endogenous UNC-93 function and cause the suppression of the rubberband Unc phenotype by uaf-1(n4588) (68% alternatively spliced unc-93 transcript), the transgene should also suppress the Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals. However, expression of the alternatively spliced unc-93 transcript in the body-wall muscles did not suppress the Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals (Table S3), suggesting that the alternatively spliced unc-93 transcript caused a loss of unc-93 function and did not interfere with endogenous unc-93 function.
###end p 34
###begin p 35
###xml 55 67 55 67 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 106 119 106 119 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 184 189 184 189 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 203 209 203 209 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 239 248 239 248 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g002">Figure 2D</xref>
###xml 253 262 253 262 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4B</xref>
###xml 340 353 340 353 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 434 443 434 443 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s002">Figure S2</xref>
###xml 460 465 460 465 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 521 534 521 534 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 567 579 567 579 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 628 640 628 640 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 786 799 786 799 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 812 822 812 822 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s3">Discussion</xref>
###xml 854 866 854 866 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 875 880 875 880 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 899 910 899 910 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(RNAi)</italic>
###xml 927 932 927 932 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
To examine whether reducing UAF-1 expression, like the uaf-1(n4588) mutation, would alter the splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9, we fed animals with bacteria expressing dsRNA targeting uaf-1 and assessed unc-93 exon 9 splicing. As shown in Figure 2D and Figure 4B, reducing UAF-1 did not increase the relative level of alternatively spliced unc-93(e1500) exon 9. The RNAi treatment did significantly reduce the level of UAF-1 protein (Figure S2). That reducing uaf-1 expression with RNAi did not cause altered splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 similarly to that by the uaf-1(n4588) mutation is consistent with the hypothesis that uaf-1(n4588) does not reduce the function of UAF-1a but rather alters the function of UAF-1a, which leads to the recognition of the cryptic 3' splice site of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 (see Discussion). However, it is possible that uaf-1(n4588) reduces uaf-1 function and that uaf-1(RNAi) does not reduce uaf-1 function as much.
###end p 35

###xml 147 159 147 159 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9(n1550)</italic>
###xml 169 176 169 176 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t001">Table 1</xref>
###xml 229 235 229 235 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 244 256 244 256 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 266 275 266 275 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s001">Figure S1</xref>
###xml 302 314 302 314 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
###xml 355 367 355 367 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 377 389 377 389 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 424 430 424 430 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 480 486 480 486 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 493 503 493 503 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s003">Figure S3A</xref>
###xml 541 547 541 547 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 585 597 585 597 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
###xml 599 611 599 611 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 616 628 616 628 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 630 642 630 642 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
###xml 699 705 699 705 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
uaf-1(n4588) suppressed the rubberband Unc phenotype of sup-10(n983) animals but did not suppress the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(n200) and sup-9(n1550) animals (Table 1). Quantitative RT-PCR did not indicate reduction of sup-10 mRNA in uaf-1(n4588) animals (Figure S1). We examined whether the sup-10(n983) transcript was alternatively spliced in uaf-1(n4588) mutants. uaf-1(n4588) did not cause the appearance of a sup-10 cDNA band different in size from the full-length sup-10 cDNA (Figure S3A). We determined the sequences of the sup-10 cDNA RT-PCR products from wild-type, sup-10(n983), uaf-1(n4588) and uaf-1(n4588); sup-10(n983) animals and failed to identify an alternatively spliced sup-10 transcript (data not shown).
###end p 36

###xml 463 473 463 473 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 513 517 513 517 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Lundquist1">[57]</xref>
###xml 518 522 518 522 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Spike1">[59]</xref>
###xml 528 540 528 540 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e669)</italic>

###xml 593 597 593 597 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Rogalski2">[60]</xref>
###xml 603 608 603 608 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">smu-1</italic>
###xml 613 618 613 618 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">smu-2</italic>
###xml 641 653 641 653 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e669)</italic>
###xml 740 744 740 744 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Spartz1">[58]</xref>
###xml 750 762 750 762 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e444)</italic>
###xml 800 806 800 806 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52</italic>
###xml 840 845 840 845 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">smu-1</italic>
###xml 850 855 850 855 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">smu-2</italic>
###xml 955 967 955 967 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e444)</italic>
###xml 985 990 985 990 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">smu-1</italic>
###xml 994 999 994 999 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">smu-2</italic>
###xml 1035 1039 1035 1039 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Spartz1">[58]</xref>
###xml 1075 1087 1075 1087 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e669)</italic>
###xml 1089 1101 1089 1101 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1106 1118 1106 1118 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e444)</italic>
###xml 1120 1132 1120 1132 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1156 1168 1156 1168 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1193 1205 1193 1205 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e669)</italic>
###xml 1209 1221 1209 1221 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e444)</italic>
###xml 1223 1231 1223 1231 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s005">Table S1</xref>
###xml 1252 1264 1252 1264 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1317 1329 1317 1329 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e669)</italic>
###xml 194 204 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 217 222 <span type="species:ncbi:9606">human</span>
###xml 463 473 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
To test whether uaf-1(n4588) can affect the splicing of all genes known to be alternatively spliced, we tested for genetic interactions between uaf-1(n4588) and unc-52(e669). unc-52 encodes the C. elegans ortholog of human basement membrane-specific heparan sulfate proteoglycan core protein, and mutations affecting unc-52 cause adult paralysis [55],[56]. The Unc phenotype of unc-52(e669) can be suppressed by lf mutations of smu-1 and smu-2, genes that encode C. elegans homologs of mammalian splicing factors [57]-[59]. The unc-52(e669) mutation causes a pre-mature stop in unc-52 exon 17 [60], and smu-1 and smu-2 lf mutations suppress unc-52(e669) by removing exon 17 and generating an alternatively spliced and functional transcript [58]. The unc-52(e444) mutation causes a pre-mature stop in unc-52 exon 18, which is not removed in smu-1 and smu-2 mutant animals, leading to a transcript with a premature stop codon. Double mutants containing the unc-52(e444) mutation and the smu-1 or smu-2 mutations display an Unc phenotype [58]. We examined the Unc phenotypes of unc-52(e669); uaf-1(n4588) and unc-52(e444); uaf-1(n4588) animals and found that uaf-1(n4588) did not suppress either unc-52(e669) or unc-52(e444) (Table S1), implying that the uaf-1(n4588) mutation did not affect the alternative splicing of unc-52(e669) exon 17 and thus does not affect all cases of alternative splicing non-specifically.
###end p 37
###begin title 38
###xml 0 5 0 5 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 32 37 32 37 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 57 67 57 67 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 57 67 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
n4562 is a nonsense mutation in sfa-1, which encodes the C. elegans ortholog of the splicing factor SF1/BBP
###end title 38
###begin p 39
###xml 13 18 13 18 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 111 124 111 124 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 178 183 178 183 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 322 343 322 343 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 351 363 351 363 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 365 370 365 370 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 382 395 382 395 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 400 412 400 412 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
###xml 434 446 434 446 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(n200)</italic>
###xml 450 462 450 462 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9(n1550)</italic>
###xml 464 471 464 471 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t001">Table 1</xref>
###xml 485 490 485 490 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 532 538 532 538 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
The mutation n4562 was also isolated from our clonal screen as a suppressor of the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals. The suppressed phenotype was recessive, and n4562 caused a completely penetrant recessive sterility that was temperature independent and was tightly linked to its suppressor activity (see Materials and Methods). Like uaf-1(n4588), n4562 suppressed unc-93(e1500) and sup-10(n983) but did not suppress unc-93(n200) or sup-9(n1550) (Table 1). Therefore, n4562 is also an allele-specific suppressor of unc-93 gf mutations but not a gene-specific suppressor for the rubberband Unc genes.
###end p 39
###begin p 40
###xml 10 15 10 15 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>

###xml 254 255 254 255 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">f</underline>
###xml 261 262 261 262 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">1</underline>

###xml 618 623 618 623 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 678 683 678 683 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-2</italic>
###xml 688 698 688 698 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Y116A8C.32</italic>
###xml 704 709 704 709 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 756 766 756 766 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Y116A8C.32</italic>
###xml 783 788 783 788 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 790 793 790 793 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa</italic>
###xml 795 796 795 796 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">s</underline>
###xml 804 806 804 806 <underline xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fa</underline>
###xml 813 822 813 822 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g003">Figure 3A</xref>
###xml 825 830 825 830 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 975 991 975 991 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g003">Figure 3A and 3B</xref>
###xml 1105 1118 1105 1118 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1122 1134 1122 1134 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 1213 1218 1213 1218 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">myo-3</italic>
###xml 1228 1232 1228 1232 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Okkema1">[49]</xref>
###xml 1234 1241 1234 1241 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t002">Table 2</xref>
###xml 1252 1265 1252 1265 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1315 1320 1315 1320 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 1372 1379 1372 1379 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t002">Table 2</xref>
###xml 163 173 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
We mapped n4562 to the right of LG IV (see Materials and Methods). No known suppressors of unc-93(e1500) are located in this region. The genes uaf-2, encoding the C. elegans U2AF small subunit ortholog [61] and Y116A8C.32, encoding the SF1/BBP (splicing factor 1/branch-point binding protein) ortholog [62], are located in this genomic region and are expressed from the same operon together with three other genes (Wormbase WS189) [61],[62]. Orthologs of UAF-2 and SF1/BBP function with the ortholog of UAF-1 to regulate pre-mRNA splicing [2], leading us to consider these two genes as candidates for being mutated by n4562. We determined the DNA sequences of coding regions of uaf-2 and Y116A8C.32 from n4562 animals and identified a nonsense mutation in Y116A8C.32, which we named sfa-1 (sfa, splicing factor) (Figure 3A). n4562 changed amino acid 458 from a Cys (TGT) to an opal stop (TGA) codon in a conserved C2HC-type zinc finger domain of the predicted SFA-1 protein (Figure 3A and 3B). This mutation is predicted to cause the expression of a truncated SFA-1 protein. We rescued the suppression of unc-93(e1500) by sfa-1(n4562) by expressing in body-wall muscles an SFA-1::GFP fusion protein driven by the myo-3 promoter [49] (Table 2). Feeding unc-93(e1500) animals with bacteria expressing dsRNA targeting sfa-1 partially suppressed the rubberband Unc phenotype (Table 2).
###end p 40

###xml 0 5 0 5 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
sfa-1 gene and protein.
###end title 41
###begin p 42
###xml 14 19 14 19 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 65 69 65 69 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Mazroui1">[62]</xref>
###xml 92 97 92 97 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 124 129 124 129 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 200 205 200 205 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>

###xml 756 769 756 769 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 802 807 802 807 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>

###end p 42
###begin p 43
###xml 15 20 15 20 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 40 45 40 45 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 127 136 123 132 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g003">Figure 3A</xref>
###xml 263 267 259 263 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Mazroui1">[62]</xref>
###xml 269 274 265 270 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 405 410 397 402 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 411 416 403 408 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 465 470 453 458 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 471 476 459 464 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 483 484 467 468 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+</italic>
###xml 534 547 518 531 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 574 587 558 571 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)/</italic>
###xml 588 593 572 577 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 696 701 676 681 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 702 707 682 687 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 743 748 719 724 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 749 754 725 730 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 805 810 777 782 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 811 816 783 788 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 827 845 795 813 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)/sfa-1</italic>
###xml 846 851 814 819 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 879 884 843 848 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 1004 1025 964 985 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
We isolated an sfa-1 deletion mutation, n5223Delta, which removes the third and fourth exons and a majority of the fifth exon (Figure 3A). Together these regions are predicted to encode most (101 aa) of the U2AF large subunit-interacting domain (118 aa) of SFA-1 [62]. n5223Delta is predicted to cause a frameshift after amino acid 188 if the second exon and the residual fifth exon are spliced together. sfa-1(n5223Delta) caused recessive embryonic lethality, and sfa-1(n5223Delta)/+ did not suppress the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals (data not shown). sfa-1(n4562)/(n5223Delta) similarly caused embryonic lethalilty (data not shown), suggesting that the lethal phenotype of sfa-1(n5223Delta) homozygotes is caused by the sfa-1(n5223Delta) mutation. The embryonic lethality caused by sfa-1(n5223Delta) and sfa-1(n4562)/sfa-1(n5223Delta) precluded the use of n5223Delta for an analysis of the rubberband Unc phenotype, because our behavioral assay is performed with young adults (see Materials and Methods).
###end p 43
###begin title 44
###xml 0 12 0 12 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 51 64 51 64 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
sfa-1(n4562) did not cause alternative splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 at the cryptic 3' splice site
###end title 44
###begin p 45
###xml 22 34 22 34 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 36 48 36 48 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 80 93 80 93 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 144 157 144 157 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 178 187 178 187 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g003">Figure 3C</xref>
###xml 192 201 192 201 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4B</xref>
###xml 203 215 203 215 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 264 277 264 277 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 310 315 310 315 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 319 332 319 332 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 361 366 361 366 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 390 399 390 399 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g003">Figure 3D</xref>
###xml 402 413 402 413 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(RNAi)</italic>
###xml 460 469 460 469 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g003">Figure 3D</xref>
###xml 474 483 474 483 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4B</xref>
To test whether, like uaf-1(n4588), sfa-1(n4562) caused alternative splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9, we used RT-PCR to examine the splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9. As shown in Figure 3C and Figure 4B, sfa-1(n4562) did not cause increased alternative splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9. We tested the effect of sfa-1 on unc-93(e1500) exon 9 splicing by reducing sfa-1 expression using RNAi (Figure 3D). sfa-1(RNAi) did not increase exon 9 alternative splicing (Figure 3D and Figure 4B).
###end p 45
###begin title 46
###xml 39 45 39 45 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
Taqman Real-time PCR quantification of unc-93 alternative splicing.

###begin p 47
###xml 104 110 104 110 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>

###begin p 48
###xml 16 28 16 28 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 146 151 146 151 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 152 157 152 157 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 193 211 189 207 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)/sfa-1</italic>
###xml 212 217 208 213 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 229 240 221 232 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(RNAi)</italic>
###xml 253 265 245 257 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 320 333 312 325 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 351 362 343 354 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(RNAi)</italic>
###xml 375 387 367 379 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 417 430 409 422 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 455 467 447 459 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 494 499 486 491 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 560 573 552 565 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 585 597 577 589 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 626 631 618 623 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
Because (1) the sfa-1(n4562) mutation causes a recessive sterile phenotype, which is less severe than the recessive embryonic lethality caused by sfa-1(n5223Delta) (likely a null allele) or by sfa-1(n4562)/sfa-1(n5223Delta), (2) sfa-1(RNAi) phenocopies sfa-1(n4562) in the suppression of the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals, and (3) sfa-1(RNAi) phenocopies sfa-1(n4562) in affecting the splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9, we propose that sfa-1(n4562) is a partial lf allele of sfa-1 and that the suppression of the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals by sfa-1(n4562) is likely caused by reduced sfa-1 function.
###end p 48
###begin p 49
###xml 19 31 19 31 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 68 81 68 81 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 103 115 103 115 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 139 151 139 151 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 153 165 153 165 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 190 203 190 203 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 210 222 210 222 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 224 236 224 236 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 262 275 262 275 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 376 385 376 385 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s004">Figure S4</xref>
To examine whether sfa-1(n4562) affects the alternative splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 caused by the uaf-1(n4588) mutation, we generated uaf-1(n4588); sfa-1(n4562) animals with or without unc-93(e1500). Most uaf-1(n4588); sfa-1(n4562) animals (with or without unc-93(e1500)) died embryonically, and the few that hatched arrested at the L2 larval stage (based on body size) (Figure S4). We failed to obtain a sufficient number of animals for RT-PCR analysis.
###end p 49
###begin p 50
###xml 17 23 17 23 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 36 48 36 48 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 106 112 106 112 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 125 135 125 135 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s003">Figure S3B</xref>
We also examined sup-10 splicing in sfa-1(n4562) animals and failed to detect alternative splicing of the sup-10 transcript (Figure S3B).
###end p 50

###end title 51
###begin p 52
###xml 20 32 20 32 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>

###xml 305 310 299 304 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5120</italic>
###xml 312 317 306 311 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5123</italic>

###xml 383 404 377 398 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
###xml 470 482 464 476 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n5123)</italic>
###xml 550 555 544 549 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 578 585 572 579 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t003">Table 3</xref>
###xml 590 598 584 592 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g005">Figure 5</xref>
###xml 659 672 653 666 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 674 681 668 675 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t004">Table 4</xref>
###xml 684 702 678 696 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588 n5120)</italic>
###xml 772 777 766 771 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 794 801 788 795 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t003">Table 3</xref>

###xml 858 871 852 865 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 873 880 867 874 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t004">Table 4</xref>
###xml 883 901 877 895 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588 n5125)</italic>
###xml 971 976 965 970 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 993 1000 987 994 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t003">Table 3</xref>
###xml 1005 1013 999 1007 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g005">Figure 5</xref>

###xml 1062 1075 1056 1069 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1077 1084 1071 1078 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t004">Table 4</xref>
###xml 1087 1105 1081 1099 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588 n5127)</italic>
###xml 1176 1181 1170 1175 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 1198 1205 1192 1199 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t003">Table 3</xref>
###xml 1210 1218 1204 1212 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g005">Figure 5</xref>
###xml 1257 1270 1251 1264 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1272 1279 1266 1273 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t004">Table 4</xref>
###xml 1291 1304 1285 1298 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1330 1348 1324 1342 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588 n5120)</italic>
###xml 1350 1368 1344 1362 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588 n5125)</italic>
###xml 1373 1391 1367 1385 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588 n5127)</italic>
###xml 1407 1412 1401 1406 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1483 1489 1477 1483 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
###xml 1491 1500 1485 1494 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g001">Figure 1A</xref>
###xml 1539 1552 1533 1546 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1592 1599 1586 1593 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="table" rid="pgen-1000708-t004">Table 4</xref>
###xml 1632 1645 1626 1639 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1681 1686 1675 1680 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1730 1739 1724 1733 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4B</xref>
###xml 1747 1752 1741 1746 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1813 1826 1807 1820 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1835 1847 1829 1841 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n5123)</italic>
###xml 1911 1924 1905 1918 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1933 1951 1927 1945 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588 n5120)</italic>
###xml 1956 1974 1950 1968 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588 n5125)</italic>
###xml 2014 2032 2008 2026 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588 n5127)</italic>
###xml 2088 2101 2082 2095 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 2110 2119 2104 2113 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4B</xref>
###xml 2190 2202 2184 2196 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 2210 2219 2204 2213 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4B</xref>
The ts-lethality of uaf-1(n4588) offered a genetic approach to seek new regulators of RNA splicing by screening for suppressors of the ts-lethal phenotype. We performed a genetic screen for suppressors of uaf-1(n4588) ts-lethality at 25degreesC. From this screen, we isolated four intragenic suppressors, n5120, n5123, n5125 and n5127 (Table 3) and seven extragenic suppressors (see Materials and Methods). To date we have characterized only the intragenic suppressors. uaf-1(n5123) caused an I180F (ATT-to-TTT) change at the same residue mutated by n4588 (T180I) (ACT-to-ATT) (Table 3 and Figure 5) and eliminated the suppression of the locomotion defect of unc-93(e1500) (Table 4). uaf-1(n4588 n5120) is predicted to cause a V179M (GTG-to-ATG) change in addition to the n4588 T180I mutation (Table 3 and Figure 5), and uaf-1(n4588 n5120) weakly suppressed unc-93(e1500) (Table 4). uaf-1(n4588 n5125) is predicted to cause a P177L (CCA-to-CTA) change in addition to the n4588 T180I mutation (Table 3 and Figure 5), and uaf-1(n4588 n5125) also weakly suppressed unc-93(e1500) (Table 4). uaf-1(n4588 n5127) is predicted to cause an M157I (ATG-to-ATA) change in addition to the n4588 T180I mutation (Table 3 and Figure 5) and was still a strong suppressor of unc-93(e1500) (Table 4). That the unc-93(e1500) suppressor activities of uaf-1(n4588 n5120), uaf-1(n4588 n5125) and uaf-1(n4588 n5127) were caused by uaf-1 mutations was confirmed by the observation that transgenes expressing uaf-1a (Figure 1A) in the body-wall muscles rescued the unc-93(e1500) suppressor phenotype of these mutants (Table 4). We quantified the splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 in animals containing these uaf-1 mutations using Taqman RT-PCR. As shown in Figure 4B, these uaf-1 mutations exhibited differential effects on the splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9. uaf-1(n5123) had no apparent effect (1.6% alternative splicing vs. 1.3% for unc-93(e1500) alone). uaf-1(n4588 n5120) and uaf-1(n4588 n5125) weakly (4% and 2.8%, respectively) and uaf-1(n4588 n5127) moderately (25%) increased the alternative splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 (Figure 4B). None of these mutations affected this splicing event as much as did uaf-1(n4588) (68%) (Figure 4B).
###end p 52

###xml 545 566 545 566 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">Materials and Methods</xref>
To confirm that the suppression of unc-93(e1500) was caused by mutations in uaf-1, transgenes that express a wild-type uaf-1a cDNA in the body-wall muscles (nEx[Pmyo-3uaf-1a cDNA::gfp]) were introduced into the strains of the genotypes indicated and independent stable transgenic lines were established and scored. For the uaf-1(n4588 n5120) unc-93(e1500), uaf-1(n4588 n5125) unc-93(e1500) and uaf-1(n4588 n5127) unc-93(e1500) genotypes, three independent lines were scored. Locomotion and the rubberband phenotype were assessed as described in Materials and Methods. SD: Standard deviation.

###begin p 59
###xml 16 28 16 28 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
