###xml 756 762 756 762 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-18</italic>
###xml 792 804 792 804 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 809 821 809 821 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 900 906 900 906 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 921 934 921 934 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 955 967 955 967 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(n200)</italic>
###xml 1000 1012 1000 1012 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
###xml 1194 1198 1194 1198 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-delaCruz1">[34]</xref>
###xml 1199 1203 1199 1203 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin1">[37]</xref>
###xml 1393 1400 1393 1400 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 1489 1494 1489 1494 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1499 1504 1499 1504 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 1567 1573 1567 1573 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1578 1584 1578 1584 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 1705 1718 1705 1718 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1722 1734 1722 1734 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
###xml 1823 1835 1823 1835 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(n200)</italic>
###xml 1839 1851 1839 1851 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9(n1550)</italic>
###xml 1864 1870 1864 1870 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-11</italic>
###xml 1875 1881 1875 1881 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-18</italic>
###xml 1971 1976 1971 1976 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1981 1986 1981 1986 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
The known suppressors of gf mutations of unc-93, sup-9 and sup-10 are of three classes. First, lf mutations in any of these three genes are recessive suppressors of the rubberband Unc phenotypes caused by gf mutations in any of these three genes, because the functions of all three genes are necessary for expression of the Unc phenotype [35],[36],[43]. Second, rare gf mutations of sup-11 are strong dominant suppressors of unc-93(e1500) and unc-93(n200) and partial recessive suppressors of sup-9(n1550) and sup-10(n983)[54]. The mechanism of sup-11 suppression is unknown. Third, lf mutations of sup-18 are strong recessive suppressors of sup-10(n983) and weak recessive suppressors of unc-93(e1500), unc-93(n200) and sup-9(n1550)[35]. The mechanism of sup-18 suppression is also unknown. uaf-1(n4588) and sfa-1(n4562) define a new class of suppressors: they are recessive and allele-specific for unc-93 gf mutations (unc-93(e1500) was suppressed, but unc-93(n200) was not) but not gene-specific (sup-10(n983) was also suppressed). Previous genetic and molecular studies from our laboratory led to the hypothesis that UNC-93, SUP-9 and SUP-10 form a protein complex in the body-wall muscles [34]-[37]. The identification of multiple suppressors of the rubberband Unc phenotype with distinct suppression patterns suggests that the presumptive UNC-93/SUP-9/SUP-10 complex could have multiple in vivo functions regulated in different ways. As mentioned above, we propose that mutations in uaf-1 and sfa-1 affect the splicing of one or more unknown genes required for unc-93 and sup-10 activity. This unknown gene might be required specifically for the expression of the rubberband Unc phenotype caused by unc-93(e1500) or sup-10(n983) but have a negligible role in the expression of the rubberband Unc phenotypes caused by unc-93(n200) or sup-9(n1550). Similarly, sup-11 and sup-18 could affect functions of the UNC-93/SUP-9/SUP-10 complex distinct from that affected by uaf-1 and sfa-1.
###end p 77
###begin title 78
###xml 0 5 0 5 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 10 15 10 15 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 71 78 71 78 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
uaf-1 and sfa-1 mutants provide new approaches for the analysis of the in vivo functions of the U2AF large subunit and SF1/BBP
###end title 78
###begin p 79
###xml 144 147 144 147 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Maniatis1">[1]</xref>
###xml 148 151 148 151 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Reed1">[2]</xref>
###xml 233 257 233 257 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Saccharomyces cerevisiae</italic>
###xml 262 287 262 287 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Schizosaccharomyces pombe</italic>
###xml 306 329 306 329 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Drosophila melanogaster</italic>
###xml 386 393 386 393 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 444 448 444 448 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Abovich1">[17]</xref>
###xml 450 454 450 454 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Abovich2">[27]</xref>
###xml 456 460 456 460 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Kanaar1">[67]</xref>
###xml 461 465 461 465 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Webb1">[70]</xref>
###xml 478 491 478 491 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">S. cerevisiae</italic>
###xml 583 587 583 587 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Abovich1">[17]</xref>
###xml 588 592 588 592 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Abovich2">[27]</xref>
###xml 609 617 609 617 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">S. pombe</italic>
###xml 627 634 627 634 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 693 697 693 697 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Potashkin1">[68]</xref>
###xml 698 702 698 702 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Webb1">[70]</xref>
###xml 707 717 707 717 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Drosophila</italic>
###xml 785 789 785 789 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Kanaar1">[67]</xref>
###xml 790 794 790 794 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Rudner2">[69]</xref>
###xml 864 874 864 874 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 903 908 903 908 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 912 917 912 917 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 943 947 943 947 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio3">[61]</xref>
###xml 948 952 948 952 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Mazroui1">[62]</xref>
###xml 1053 1058 1053 1058 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1063 1068 1063 1068 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 1332 1339 1332 1339 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 226 232 <span type="species:ncbi:4932">yeasts</span>
###xml 233 257 <span type="species:ncbi:4932">Saccharomyces cerevisiae</span>
###xml 262 287 <span type="species:ncbi:4896">Schizosaccharomyces pombe</span>
###xml 296 305 <span type="species:ncbi:7227">fruit fly</span>
###xml 306 329 <span type="species:ncbi:7227">Drosophila melanogaster</span>
###xml 478 491 <span type="species:ncbi:4932">S. cerevisiae</span>
###xml 609 617 <span type="species:ncbi:4896">S. pombe</span>
###xml 864 874 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
The SF1/BBP and U2AF proteins are critical splicing factors that regulate splicing by binding the branch-point sequence and the 3' splice sites [1],[2], respectively. Mutations that affect the U2AF subunits and SF1/BBP in the yeasts Saccharomyces cerevisiae and Schizosaccharomyces pombe and the fruit fly Drosophila melanogaster have significantly facilitated the understanding of the in vivo function and regulation of these splicing factors [17], [27], [67]-[70]. Studies of S. cerevisiae identified genetic and biochemical interactions between the U2AF large subunit and SF1/BBP [17],[27], and studies of S. pombe provided in vivo evidence that the U2AF subunits are required for splicing [68],[70]. In Drosophila null mutations of the U2AF large or small subunits cause lethality [67],[69], hindering genetic analysis of these splicing factors. Similarly, in C. elegans, reducing the expression of uaf-1 or sfa-1 by RNAi causes lethality [61],[62], suggesting that these genes are essential for animal survival. We identified mutations that affect uaf-1 and sfa-1 and allow the survival of animals in permissive conditions, such as at lower temperatures or when derived from heterozygous mothers. These mutations provide a valuable resource for analyzing the function and regulation of the U2AF large subunit and SF1/BBP genes in vivo in animals.
###end p 79
###begin title 80
###xml 29 36 29 36 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
Mutations in UAF-1 alter the in vivo recognition of a 3' splice site
###end title 80
###begin p 81
###xml 166 169 166 169 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Maniatis1">[1]</xref>
###xml 170 173 170 173 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Reed1">[2]</xref>
###xml 321 328 321 328 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
The recognition of 3' splice sites is achieved by interactions between SF1/BBP and the U2AF large and small subunits, which together bind specific intronic sequences [1],[2]. However, it is not clear how these factors regulate the choice of the correct splice site when two or more potential 3' splice sites are proximal in vivo. Distinguishing different 3' splice sites is a critical aspect of alternative splicing.
###end p 81
###begin p 82
###xml 4 17 4 17 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 100 101 100 101 <bold xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">a</bold>
###xml 161 171 161 171 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 182 186 182 186 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Hollins1">[29]</xref>
###xml 214 224 214 224 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 294 302 294 302 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s008">Table S4</xref>
###xml 314 322 314 322 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vitro</italic>
###xml 461 465 461 465 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Hollins1">[29]</xref>
###xml 545 558 545 558 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 606 619 606 619 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 752 757 752 757 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 779 784 779 784 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1036 1043 1036 1043 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 161 171 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
###xml 214 224 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
The unc-93(e1500) missense mutation generates a new cryptic 3' splice site (AG) within exon 9 (ACTGcag). This site differs from the consensus 3' splice site for C. elegans (TTTTcag) [29] and is more rarely used by C. elegans than is TTTTcag or the intron 8 endogenous 3' splice site (AATTcag) (Table S4). Based on in vitro studies, this cryptic site should not be or be more weakly recognized by UAF-1 compared to TTTTcag and probably the intron 8 site AATTcag [29]. In a wild-type background, the choice between the wild-type 3' splice site of unc-93(e1500) intron 8 and the cryptic non-consensus site in unc-93(e1500) exon 9 followed this prediction, as only 1.3% of the splicing events utilized this cryptic 3' splice site. Strikingly, however, the n4588 missense mutation in uaf-1 shifted this specificity, causing splicing to occur mostly at the cryptic site, generating 68% of aberrantly spliced transcripts. This result suggests that UAF-1 might play an important role in determining the choice among alternative 3' splice sites in vivo (see discussion below).
###end p 82
###begin p 83
###xml 4 9 4 9 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 192 204 192 204 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 298 307 298 307 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s002">Figure S2</xref>
###xml 383 396 383 396 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 493 506 493 506 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 517 543 517 543 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 641 653 641 653 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 786 799 786 799 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 836 849 836 849 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
The n4588 mutation did not cause an apparent change of UAF-1 protein level, and reducing UAF-1 using RNAi did not increase the relative amount of alternatively spliced exon 9, suggesting that uaf-1(n4588) might alter UAF-1 function. However, RNAi-treatment did not abolish the expression of UAF-1 (Figure S2), and we might have failed to detect an effect of UAF-1 on the splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 because of residual UAF-1 protein in RNAi-treated animals. Thus, the altered splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 in uaf-1(n4588) unc-93(e1500) mutants might reflect the consequence of the absence of UAF-1 activity. It is also possible that uaf-1(n4588) causes both a loss of function and an altered function of UAF-1, which cause the suppression of the rubberband Unc phenotype of the unc-93(e1500) animals and the altered splicing of unc-93(e1500) transcript, respectively.
###end p 83
###begin p 84
###xml 28 34 28 34 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 96 108 96 108 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 134 146 134 146 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 231 243 231 243 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 293 305 293 305 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e669)</italic>
###xml 382 387 382 387 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">smu-1</italic>
###xml 392 397 392 397 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">smu-2</italic>
###xml 420 432 420 432 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
The other 14 introns of the unc-93 transcript appeared to be spliced similarly in wild-type and uaf-1(n4588) animals, suggesting that uaf-1(n4588) did not alter the recognition of most wild-type 3' splice sites. We also found that uaf-1(n4588) did not suppress the Unc phenotype caused by the unc-52(e669) mutation, which can be suppressed by mutations in the splicing factor genes smu-1 and smu-2. We conclude that the uaf-1(n4588) mutation does not affect all cases in which alternative splicing is possible.
###end p 84
###begin p 85
###xml 89 101 89 101 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 129 140 129 140 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588 n5120</italic>
###xml 142 153 142 153 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588 n5125</italic>
###xml 158 169 158 169 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588 n5127</italic>
###xml 197 202 197 202 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 242 247 242 247 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 265 270 265 270 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 317 330 317 330 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 378 390 378 390 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 535 540 535 540 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5123</italic>
###xml 581 586 581 586 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 715 720 715 720 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 748 760 748 760 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n5123)</italic>
###xml 785 793 785 793 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(+)</italic>
###xml 908 913 908 913 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 925 930 925 930 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 932 937 932 937 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5120</italic>
###xml 939 944 939 944 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5123</italic>
###xml 946 951 946 951 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5125</italic>
###xml 956 961 956 961 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5127</italic>
###xml 1038 1042 1038 1042 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Rudner1">[47]</xref>
###xml 1068 1072 1068 1072 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zamore3">[26]</xref>
###xml 1073 1077 1073 1077 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio2">[45]</xref>
###xml 1079 1087 1079 1087 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g005">Figure 5</xref>
We isolated four intragenic suppressors of the temperature-sensitive lethality caused by uaf-1(n4588). Three of the suppressors (n4588 n5120, n4588 n5125 and n4588 n5127) carried both the original n4588 mutation and a second site mutation in uaf-1. These three new uaf-1 mutations reduced the alternative splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9 to levels intermediate between those of uaf-1(n4588) and wild-type animals. This finding supports the hypothesis that UAF-1 is important in 3' splice-site choice. The fourth intragenic suppressor, n5123, affected the same site as the original n4588 mutation by generating a phenylalanine codon different from both the wild-type codon (threonine) and the codon generated by the n4588 mutation (isoleucine). The uaf-1(n5123) allele behaves like the uaf-1(+) allele, suggesting that this mutation restored the normal specificity of UAF-1. The amino acids affected by these uaf-1 mutations (n4588, n5120, n5123, n5125 and n5127) are confined to a region between the U2AF small subunit-interacting domain [47] and the first RRM domain [26],[45] (Figure 5). We postulate that this region of UAF-1 defines a domain of UAF-1 important for 3' splice-site selection.
###end p 85
###begin title 86
The sequences and positions of 3' splice sites together define the efficiency of splicing events
###end title 86
###begin p 87
###xml 3 13 3 13 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 123 127 123 127 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Hollins1">[29]</xref>
###xml 128 132 128 132 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Kent1">[64]</xref>
###xml 179 183 179 183 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Hollins1">[29]</xref>
###xml 273 280 273 280 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 3 13 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
In C. elegans, the first two nucleotides (-2 to -1) of 3' splice sites are more highly conserved than nucleotides -7 to -3 [29],[64], which affect the binding of the U2AF factors [29]. We sought to identify the nucleotides that affect the recognition of I8 and E9 by UAF-1 in vivo.
###end p 87
###begin p 88
###xml 244 253 244 253 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g006">Figure 6B</xref>
###xml 484 492 484 492 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g006">Figure 6</xref>
###xml 618 628 618 628 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 706 714 706 714 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s008">Table S4</xref>
###xml 1200 1212 1200 1212 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1286 1292 1286 1292 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1294 1303 1294 1303 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g002">Figure 2B</xref>
###xml 618 628 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
First, we conclude that the location of a 3' splice site affects its recognition. We found that the location of E9 was preferred to that of I8 by both wild-type and mutant UAF-1 when identical 3' splice sites were present at the two locations (Figure 6B, No. 2 and 3). However, this positional effect was not absolute. When the high-affinity 3' splice site TTTTcag was placed at either of the two locations, the site with the TTTTcag was preferred by both wild-type and mutant UAF-1 (Figure 6, No. 6 and No. 12). That splicing using I8 and E9 (both are likely weak 3' splice sites, since there are fewer such sites in C. elegans introns than there are copies of the strong 3' splice site sequence TTTTcag (Table S4)) was more affected by position than was splicing using the sequence TTTTcag suggests that weak 3' splice sites might be preferably used for alternative splicing, and, strong 3' splice sites such as TTTTcag might be generally used for constitutive splicing. If so, we might identify alternatively spliced genes by searching apparently weak 3' splice sites and then performing RT-PCR analyses. That TTTTcag is strongly recognized by mutant UAF-1 is consistent with our finding that the uaf-1(n4588) mutation does not appear to affect the splicing of most other introns of unc-93 (Figure 2B), which have a 3' splice site identical or highly similar to TTTTcag (data not shown).
###end p 88
###begin p 89
###xml 157 165 157 165 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g006">Figure 6</xref>
###xml 434 442 434 442 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g006">Figure 6</xref>
Second, we conclude that the nucleotides at -7, -5 and -4 were more important than the nucleotide at -6 for wild-type UAF-1 to recognize the sequence of I8 (Figure 6, No. 7 to No. 10). The nucleotides at -4 and -5 appear to be more important than that at -7. That the nucleotide at -4 is more important than the nucleotide at -6 also appears to be the case for splicing at E9 by wild-type UAF-1 (No. 15 and No. 16, compared to No. 2, Figure 6), which indicates that nucleotide substitution at -4 (No. 16) dramatically reduced splicing and nucleotide substitution at -6 (No. 15) had a minimal effect at E9 in wild-type animals.
###end p 89
###begin p 90
###xml 320 330 320 330 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 332 340 332 340 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s008">Table S4</xref>
###xml 342 346 342 346 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Hollins1">[29]</xref>
###xml 347 351 347 351 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Kent1">[64]</xref>
###xml 405 413 405 413 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s008">Table S4</xref>
###xml 575 583 575 583 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g006">Figure 6</xref>
###xml 741 749 741 749 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g006">Figure 6</xref>
###xml 320 330 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
Third, substituting individual non-T nucleotides with T in E9 improved its recognition by wild-type UAF-1. The original I8 (AATTcag) and E9 (ACTGcag) are both rare 3' splice sites compared to TTTTcag, which is found in about 26% of the approximate 40000 introns analyzed, and is the most commonly used 3' splice site in C. elegans (Table S4) [29],[64]. I8 appears more frequently in introns than does E9 (Table S4), suggesting that E9 has a lower affinity for the wild-type UAF-1 than does I8. That the wild-type UAF-1 rarely recognized E9 even in the more favored position (Figure 6, No. 1) is consistent with this notion. We found that substituting any E9 non-T nucleotide with T could increase the recognition of E9 in wild-type animals (Figure 6, No. 13 to 15), and a T substitution at -6 and -4 had a much stronger effect than one at -7.
###end p 90
###begin p 91
###xml 35 40 35 40 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 292 304 292 304 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 314 322 314 322 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g006">Figure 6</xref>
###xml 457 469 457 469 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
Fourth, we conclude that the T180I(n4588) mutation caused UAF-1 to be more tolerant of a G nucleotide at -4 of E9. In transgenes No. 11 and No. 16, a G substitution at -4 of E9 dramatically reduced splicing at E9 in wild-type animals but did not or only moderately affected splicing at E9 in uaf-1(n4588) mutants (Figure 6). The splicing of transgenes No. 1, No. 4 and No. 5 is consistent with this observation, implying that a G at -4 is more tolerated in uaf-1(n4588) animals than in wild-type animals. Based on these observations, we propose that the G nucleotide at position -4 of E9 is critical for its recognition by the mutant UAF-1.
###end p 91
###begin title 92
###xml 0 7 0 7 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">In vivo</italic>
In vivo functions of UAF-1 and SFA-1 probably remain to be discovered
###end title 92
###begin p 93
###xml 0 7 0 7 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">In vivo</italic>
###xml 118 128 118 128 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Drosophila</italic>
###xml 279 283 279 283 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Blanchette1">[71]</xref>
###xml 483 491 483 491 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vitro</italic>
###xml 495 502 495 502 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 565 569 565 569 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Guth1">[72]</xref>
###xml 574 587 574 587 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">S. cerevisiae</italic>
###xml 587 591 587 591 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Rutz1">[73]</xref>
###xml 641 654 641 654 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">S. cerevisiae</italic>
###xml 654 658 654 658 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Rutz1">[73]</xref>
###xml 697 705 697 705 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vitro</italic>
###xml 834 838 834 838 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Tanackovic1">[74]</xref>
###xml 845 857 845 857 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 862 874 862 874 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 907 920 907 920 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 966 979 966 979 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1029 1034 1029 1034 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1039 1044 1039 1044 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 1081 1088 1081 1088 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 1102 1112 1102 1112 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 1186 1191 1186 1191 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1196 1201 1196 1201 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 1280 1292 1280 1292 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 1334 1347 1334 1347 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1362 1374 1362 1374 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 574 587 <span type="species:ncbi:4932">S. cerevisiae</span>
###xml 641 654 <span type="species:ncbi:4932">S. cerevisiae</span>
###xml 1102 1112 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
In vivo studies have suggested functions for the U2AF large subunit beyond regulating pre-mRNA splicing. For example, Drosophila mutants with a temperature-sensitive U2AF large subunit are defective in the nucleus-to-cytoplasm export of intronless mRNAs at elevated temperatures [71], suggesting that lack of U2AF large subunit function can affect mRNA export in addition to pre-mRNA splicing. Studies of SF1/BBP suggest that this splicing factor might not be essential for splicing in vitro or in vivo. Biochemical depletion of SF1/BBP in extracts from HeLa cells [72] and S. cerevisiae[73] or genetic depletion of SF1/BBP in extracts from S. cerevisiae[73] did not significantly affect splicing in vitro. Reducing SF1/BBP expression by RNAi in HeLa cells does not affect the splicing of several endogenous genes and a reporter gene [74]. That uaf-1(n4588) and sfa-1(n4562) suppressed the Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) but had different effects on the splicing of unc-93(e1500) mRNA at the cryptic 3' splice site suggests that uaf-1 and sfa-1 could have both distinct and shared in vivo functions in C. elegans. Specifically, the splicing of some genes might be affected similarly by uaf-1 and sfa-1, with other genes differentially affected. Alternatively, it is possible that uaf-1(n4588) has a stronger effect on the splicing of unc-93(e1500) exon 9, while sfa-1(n4562) has a weaker effect not detected in the experiments we performed.
###end p 93
###begin p 94
###xml 111 118 111 118 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 264 271 264 271 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 359 369 359 369 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 426 433 426 433 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 359 369 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
The lack of conditionally viable mutants of the U2AF large subunit and SF1/BBP has impeded the analysis of the in vivo functions of these splicing factors in animals. The mutations we isolated affecting these two splicing factors should allow novel approaches for in vivo analyses of RNA splicing and of the functions of the U2AF large subunit and SF1/BBP in C. elegans. The transgene splicing system we developed provides an in vivo reporter assay for understanding the role of UAF-1 and possibly other splicing factors in regulating alternative 3' splice site recognition.
###end p 94
###begin title 95
Materials and Methods
###end title 95
###begin title 96
Strains
###end title 96
###begin p 97
###xml 0 10 0 10 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">C. elegans</italic>
###xml 57 61 51 55 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Brenner1">[55]</xref>
###xml 231 235 225 229 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Wicks1">[75]</xref>
###xml 280 292 274 286 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-11(n403)</italic>
###xml 292 296 286 290 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald3">[54]</xref>
###xml 304 323 298 317 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9(n1550, n2287)</italic>
###xml 323 327 317 321 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-delaCruz1">[34]</xref>
###xml 328 332 322 326 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin2">[43]</xref>
###xml 334 352 328 346 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e444, e669)</italic>
###xml 352 356 346 350 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Brenner1">[55]</xref>
###xml 357 361 351 355 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Rogalski2">[60]</xref>
###xml 370 381 364 375 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">vab-6(e697)</italic>
###xml 386 395 380 389 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">dpy-1(e1)</italic>
###xml 395 399 389 393 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Brenner1">[55]</xref>
###xml 401 406 395 400 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 407 412 401 406 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 414 419 408 413 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5120</italic>
###xml 421 426 415 420 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5123</italic>
###xml 428 433 422 427 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5125</italic>
###xml 435 440 429 434 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5127</italic>
###xml 442 447 436 441 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 468 500 458 490 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(lr12, n200, n1912, e1500)</italic>
###xml 500 504 490 494 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald2">[36]</xref>
###xml 505 509 495 499 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin1">[37]</xref>
###xml 510 514 500 504 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-DeStasio1">[44]</xref>
###xml 516 529 506 519 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-18(n1014)</italic>
###xml 529 533 519 523 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald1">[35]</xref>
###xml 541 555 531 545 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">egl-23(n601sd)</italic>
###xml 555 559 545 549 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Trent1">[52]</xref>
###xml 561 573 551 563 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">dpy-4(e1166)</italic>
###xml 573 577 563 567 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Brenner1">[55]</xref>
###xml 579 584 569 574 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 585 590 575 580 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 592 597 582 587 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
###xml 623 638 609 624 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">twk-18(e1913sd)</italic>
###xml 638 642 624 628 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Kunkel1">[53]</xref>
###xml 644 658 630 644 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-58(e665sd)</italic>
###xml 658 662 644 648 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Park1">[51]</xref>
###xml 667 686 653 672 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983, n3564)</italic>
###xml 686 690 672 676 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-delaCruz1">[34]</xref>
###xml 691 695 677 681 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Greenwald1">[35]</xref>
###xml 715 718 701 704 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">nT1</italic>
###xml 742 745 728 731 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gfp</italic>
###xml 753 758 739 744 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">qIs51</italic>
###xml 758 762 744 748 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Belfiore1">[76]</xref>
###xml 787 792 773 778 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 822 846 808 832 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sC1(s2023)[dpy-1(s2170)]</italic>
###xml 936 941 922 927 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 942 947 928 933 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 0 10 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">C. elegans</span>
C. elegans strains were grown at 20degreesC as described [55], except where otherwise specified. N2 (Bristol) was the reference wild-type strain. CB4856 (Hawaii) was used for mapping mutations using single-nucleotide polymorphisms [75]. Mutations used in this study include: LGI: sup-11(n403)[54]. LGII: sup-9(n1550, n2287)[34],[43], unc-52(e444, e669)[55],[60]. LGIII: vab-6(e697) and dpy-1(e1)[55], uaf-1(n4588, n5120, n5123, n5125, n5127, n5222Delta) (this study), unc-93(lr12, n200, n1912, e1500)[36],[37],[44], sup-18(n1014)[35]. LGIV: egl-23(n601sd)[52], dpy-4(e1166)[55], sfa-1(n4562, n5223Delta) (this study). LGX: twk-18(e1913sd)[53], unc-58(e665sd)[51] and sup-10(n983, n3564)[34],[35]. The translocation nT1 IV;V with the dominant gfp marker qIs51[76] was used to balance the sfa-1 locus, and the translocation sC1(s2023)[dpy-1(s2170)] (A. Rose, D. Baillie and D. Riddle, the Genetic Toolkit project) was used to balance the uaf-1(n5222Delta) locus.
###end p 97
###begin title 98
###xml 26 39 26 39 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
Clonal screen to identify unc-93(e1500) suppressor genes essential for animal survival
###end title 98
###begin p 99
###xml 16 29 16 29 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 40 41 40 41 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">0</sub>
###xml 107 111 107 111 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Brenner1">[55]</xref>
###xml 114 115 114 115 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">1</sub>
###xml 236 237 236 237 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">2</sub>
###xml 362 363 350 351 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">1</sub>
###xml 689 694 677 682 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 713 718 701 706 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 723 728 711 716 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4564</italic>
###xml 780 785 768 773 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4564</italic>
Synchronized L4 unc-93(e1500) animals (P0) were mutagenized with EMS (ethyl methanesulfonate) as described [55]. F1 progeny from these animals were picked to single wells of 24-well culture plates with OP50 bacteria grown on NGM agar. F2 progeny were observed using a dissecting microscope to identify animals with improved locomotion. From approximately10,000 F1 clones screened, 100 independent suppressed strains were isolated. 97 of the isolates, including two weak recessive sterile suppressors and 95 recessive fertile suppressors, were kept as frozen stocks for possible later study. Three stronger suppressors that caused or were closely linked to mutations that caused sterility (n4562) or ts-lethality (n4588 and n4564) were chosen for further analysis. The analysis of n4564 is ongoing.
###end p 99
###begin title 100
###xml 11 16 11 16 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 21 26 21 26 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
Cloning of n4588 and n4562
###end title 100
###begin p 101
###xml 10 15 10 15 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 31 36 31 36 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">dpy-1</italic>
###xml 74 87 74 87 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 182 186 182 186 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">e.g.</italic>
###xml 202 237 202 237 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588 unc-93(e1500)/+ unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 353 358 353 358 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 370 375 370 375 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 550 567 550 567 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">vab-6(e697) n4588</italic>
###xml 623 627 623 627 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Wicks1">[75]</xref>
###xml 750 765 750 765 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588 dpy-1(e1)</italic>
###xml 891 896 891 896 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 898 904 898 904 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rab-18</italic>
###xml 906 911 906 911 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">kbp-4</italic>
###xml 916 921 916 921 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">par-2</italic>
###xml 983 989 983 989 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1a</italic>
We mapped n4588 to the left of dpy-1 on LGIII based on the suppression of unc-93(e1500) using standard methods. As the suppressor activity and ts-lethality were very closely linked, e.g., more than 500 n4588 unc-93(e1500)/+ unc-93(e1500) individuals failed to segregate Sup non-Let progeny, we then followed the phenotype of ts-lethality to further map n4588. We mapped n4588 to the right of nucleotide 186577 on BE0003N10 (cosmid BE0003N10 sequences refer to nucleotides of accession no. AC092690) using 10 Vab recombinants recovered after crossing vab-6(e697) n4588 hemaphrodites with males of the Hawaiian strain CB4856 [75] and to the left of nucleotide 13164 on Y92C3A (accession no. AC024874) using 37 Dpy recombinants recovered after crossing n4588 dpy-1(e1) hemaphrodites with males from the Hawaiian strain CB4856. We determined the coding sequences of four genes in this interval, uaf-1, rab-18, kbp-4 and par-2, and identified a missense mutation in the third exon of the uaf-1a isoform.
###end p 101
###begin p 102
###xml 44 49 44 49 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 76 80 76 80 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">e.g.</italic>
###xml 91 104 91 104 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 106 113 106 113 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562/+</italic>
###xml 210 215 210 215 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 232 237 232 237 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">dpy-4</italic>
###xml 286 291 286 291 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4562</italic>
###xml 412 430 412 430 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">dpy-4(e1166) n4562</italic>
###xml 506 511 506 511 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 516 521 516 521 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-2</italic>
###xml 626 631 626 631 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
As the suppressor activity and sterility of n4562 were very closely linked, e.g., over 500 unc-93(e1500); n4562/+ individuals failed to segregate Sup non-Ste progeny, we followed the sterility phenotype to map n4562 to the right of dpy-4 on LG IV using standard methods. We next mapped n4562 to the right of nucleotide 37163 on Y43D4A (accession no. AL132846) using 234 Dpy recombinants recovered after crossing dpy-4(e1166) n4562 with males of the Hawaiian strain CB4856. The sequences of coding exons of sfa-1 and uaf-2, both located in this region, were determined, and a Cys458Opal (TGT-to-TGA) mutation was identified in sfa-1.
###end p 102
###begin title 103
Isolation of deletion alleles
###end title 103
###begin p 104
###xml 98 102 98 102 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Jansen1">[77]</xref>
###xml 216 221 216 221 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 222 227 222 227 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5222</italic>
###xml 283 288 279 284 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 289 294 285 290 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5223</italic>
Genomic DNA pools from EMS-mutagenized animals were screened for deletions using PCR as described [77]. Deletion mutant animals were isolated from frozen stocks and backcrossed to the wild type at least three times. uaf-1(n5222Delta) removes nucleotides 9786 to 11082 of YAC Y92C3B. sfa-1(n5223Delta) removes nucleotides 207818 to 208925 of YAC Y116A8C.
###end p 104
###begin title 105
Quantitative RT-PCR
###end title 105
###begin p 106
###xml 787 799 773 785 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 855 861 841 847 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rpl-26</italic>
###xml 863 868 849 854 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">gpd-2</italic>
###xml 870 875 856 861 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">act-1</italic>
###xml 895 900 881 886 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">myo-3</italic>
###xml 902 908 888 894 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 910 915 896 901 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 917 923 903 909 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 925 931 911 917 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-11</italic>
###xml 933 939 919 925 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-18</italic>
###xml 1066 1075 1052 1061 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000708-g004">Figure 4A</xref>
###xml 1321 1327 1307 1313 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">rpl-26</italic>
###xml 1332 1338 1318 1324 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1559 1567 1545 1553 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s009">Table S5</xref>
Total RNA was prepared using Trizol according to the manufacture's instructions (Invitrogen), treated with RNase-Free DNase I (New England Biolabs) and followed by incubation at 75degreesC for 10 minutes to inactivate DNase I. First-strand cDNA was synthesized with random hexamer primers (New England Biolabs) using the Superscript II or III First-Strand Synthesis Kit (Invitrogen). Quantitative RT-PCR was performed using either a DNA Engine Opticon System (MJ Research) or a Mastercycler realplex system (Eppendorf). For the SYBR green-based assay (DNA Engine Opticon System), each 30 microl PCR reaction contained 1 to 10 ng RT template, 0.5 mM PCR primers and 15 microl 2x SYBR Green PCR Master Mix (Applied Biosystems). Three independent samples of synchronized wild-type (N2) and uaf-1(n4588) L1 animals were prepared, and levels of control genes (rpl-26, gpd-2, act-1) and tested genes (myo-3, unc-93, sup-9, sup-10, sup-11, sup-18) were quantified from each biological replicate. For the Taqman probe-based assay (Mastercycler realplex system), the probes (Figure 4A) were labeled at their 5'-ends with 6-carboxyfluorescein (FAM) and at their 3'-ends with Black Hole Quencher (BHQ-1) (Integrated DNA Technologies). Two independent samples of each genotype of animals of mixed stages were prepared, and levels of rpl-26 and unc-93 wild-type and alternatively spliced transcripts were quantified from each biological replicate. For RNAi-treated animals (see below), one sample for each assay was quantified. PCR primers and Taqman probes are listed in Table S5.
###end p 106
###begin title 107
###xml 26 38 26 38 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
Screen for suppressors of uaf-1(n4588)
###end title 107
###begin p 108
###xml 13 25 13 25 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 36 37 36 37 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">0</sub>
###xml 121 125 115 119 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Brenner1">[55]</xref>
###xml 134 135 128 129 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">0</sub>
###xml 236 237 224 225 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">1</sub>
###xml 312 316 300 304 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-1">[78]</xref>
###xml 323 324 311 312 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">1</sub>
###xml 641 642 593 594 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">2</sub>
###xml 666 667 618 619 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">1</sub>
###xml 712 713 664 665 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">0</sub>
###xml 781 782 733 734 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">2</sub>
###xml 810 811 762 763 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">1</sub>
###xml 921 926 873 878 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5120</italic>
###xml 936 941 888 893 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5123</italic>
###xml 967 972 919 924 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5125</italic>
###xml 985 990 937 942 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5127</italic>
###xml 1046 1051 998 1003 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n5125</italic>
###xml 1089 1090 1041 1042 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">0</sub>
###xml 1119 1120 1071 1072 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">0</sub>
###xml 1242 1246 1194 1198 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">i.e.</italic>
###xml 1248 1255 1200 1207 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588/+</italic>
###xml 1257 1262 1209 1214 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup/+</italic>
###xml 1282 1287 1234 1239 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">n4588</italic>
###xml 1380 1381 1332 1333 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">0</sub>
Synchronized uaf-1(n4588) animals (P0) at the L4 larval stage grown at 15degreesC were mutagenized with EMS as described [55]. These P0 animals were allowed to grow to young adults at 15degreesC in a mixed population and bleached, and F1 progeny were synchronized at the early L1 stage by starvation in S medium [78]. The F1 animals were placed on 50 Petri plates (approximately1000 animals/plate) with NGM agar seeded with OP50 and permitted to grow to young adults at 15degreesC and then moved to 25degreesC. After six days at 25degreesC, the animals were grown at 20degreesC for six days and examined each day for the presence of living F2 animals. About 50,000 F1 progeny from a mixture of more than 10,000 P0 animals were screened. From the screen, we recovered 13 surviving F2 animals from 13 different F1 plates. Six of the 13 suppressors were intragenic suppressors representing four different mutations: one was n5120, one was n5123, three were identical to n5125 and one was n5127. It is possible that the three isolates containing the n5125 mutation were derived from the same P0 animal, because all of the P0 animals were in a mixed population when bleached to release eggs. The other seven suppressors were extragenic mutations, i.e., n4588/+; sup/+ animals segregated n4588-like progeny. Some or all of the extragenic isolates could have been derived from the same P0 animal.
###end p 108
###begin title 109
RNA interference
###end title 109
###begin p 110
###xml 34 47 34 47 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 150 155 150 155 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 159 164 159 164 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 219 223 219 223 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Timmons1">[79]</xref>
###xml 236 237 236 237 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">1</sub>
###xml 253 266 253 266 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 397 398 397 398 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">2</sub>
###xml 609 614 609 614 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 676 681 676 681 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
###xml 728 732 728 732 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Kamath1">[80]</xref>
###xml 842 847 842 847 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1</italic>
Young adult animals (wild-type or unc-93(e1500)) were fed HT115(DE3) bacteria containing plasmids directing the expression of dsRNAs targeting either uaf-1 or sfa-1 on NGM plates with 1 mM IPTG and 0.1 mg/ml Ampicillin [79]. Surviving F1 progeny of the unc-93(e1500) animals (escapers) were examined for suppression of locomotion defects. Animals were washed from plates, rinsed three times with H2O, and resuspended in Trizol (Invitrogen) for preparation of total RNA or in 2x protein loading buffer (see Western blots, below) for SDS-PAGE analysis. We generated the DNA construct expressing dsRNA targeting uaf-1 (see below). The bacterial strain expressing dsRNA targeting sfa-1 was obtained from a whole-genome RNAi library [80], and the sequences of plasmids from single colonies of the strain were determined to confirm the presence of sfa-1 coding sequences.
###end p 110
###begin title 111
Quantification of locomotion and the rubberband phenotype
###end title 111
###begin p 112
###xml 261 265 255 259 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Sawin1">[81]</xref>
###xml 316 320 310 314 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Levin2">[43]</xref>
L4 animals were picked 16-24 hrs before assaying and were grown at 20degreesC. Young adults were then individually picked to Petri plates containing NGM agar seeded with OP50, and bodybends were counted for 30 seconds using a dissecting microscope as described [81]. The rubberband phenotype was scored as described [43].
###end p 112
###begin title 113
Western blots
###end title 113
###begin p 114
###xml 38 39 38 39 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">2</sub>
###xml 67 68 67 68 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">2</sub>
###xml 763 767 763 767 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Zorio2">[45]</xref>
###xml 736 742 <span type="species:ncbi:9986">rabbit</span>
###xml 807 811 <span type="species:ncbi:9925">goat</span>
###xml 817 823 <span type="species:ncbi:9986">rabbit</span>
Animals were washed from plates with H2O, rinsed three times with H2O, resuspended in one volume of 2x SDS loading buffer (100 mM Tris.Cl (pH 6.8), 200 mM DTT, 4% SDS, 0.2% bromophenol blue, 20% glycerol), boiled for 5 minutes, and samples were then loaded onto 8% polyacrylamide gels containing SDS. Protein samples were transferred from polyacrylamide gels to Immobilon-P Transfer Membranes (Millipore). Primary and secondary antibody incubations were performed with 5% non-fat milk in TBST (25 mM Tris-HCl, PH 8.0; 125 mM NaCl; 0.1% Tween-20) at room temperature for one hour each. Signals were visualized using Chemiluminescence Reagent Plus (PerkinElmer Life Sciences) and X-ray film (BioMax XAR film, Kodak). Primary antibody was rabbit anti-UAF-1(1:20000) [45]. Secondary antibody was HRP-conjugated goat anti-rabbit (1:3000) (BioRad).
###end p 114

###xml 920 932 912 924 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 1012 1025 1004 1017 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1032 1045 1024 1037 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1083 1087 1075 1079 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">BamH</italic>
###xml 1100 1103 1092 1095 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Age</italic>
###xml 1322 1335 1314 1327 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 1381 1385 1373 1377 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">BamH</italic>
###xml 1391 1394 1383 1386 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Age</italic>
###xml 1419 1424 1411 1416 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">myo-3</italic>
###xml 1470 1476 1462 1468 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1483 1486 1475 1478 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Pml</italic>
###xml 1492 1496 1484 1488 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">BamH</italic>
###xml 1524 1529 1516 1521 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 1548 1554 1540 1546 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 1556 1561 1548 1553 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">e1500</italic>
###xml 1932 1940 1924 1932 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000708.s009">Table S5</xref>
To rescue the suppression of the Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) by uaf-1(n4588) or sfa-1(n4562), uaf-1 and sfa-1 cDNAs were subcloned to vector pPD93.97 using BamHI and AgeI restrictions sites. uaf-1b cDNA was amplified with PCR using uaf-1a cDNA as template and subcloned to pPD93.97 using BamHI and AgeI restrictions sites. uaf-1a cDNA was subcloned to pPD49.83 (for heat-shock induced expression of uaf-1a cDNA) using BamHI and SacI restriction sites. An XhoI/SpeI fragment of uaf-1a cDNA subcloned in a pGEM-TA easy vector (Promega) was subcloned to pPD129.36 (for the uaf-1 RNAi construct) using XhoI and NheI sites. To test whether the truncated unc-93(Delta) cDNA caused by altered splicing of the unc-93(e1500) transcript in uaf-1(n4588) mutants encodes a functional UNC-93 protein, unc-93 cDNA and unc-93(Delta) cDNA were subcloned to pPD93.97 using BamHI(blunt) and AgeI sites. To test whether uaf-1(n4588) or sfa-1(n4562) mutations could suppress the Unc phenotype caused by ectopic expression of the unc-93(e1500) cDNA, unc-93(e1500) cDNA was subcloned to pPD93.97 using BamHI(blunt) and AgeI sites. To examine the effect of nucleotide substitutions on the recognition of the intron 8 endogenous 3' splice site and the exon 9 cryptic 3' splice site, we fused the genomic sequence between exon 8 and exon 10 of unc-93(e1500) in-frame with the GFP gene of pPD93.97 using BamHI and AgeI sites. We replaced the myo-3 promoter of pPD93.97 with a 2 kb promoter of unc-93 using PmlI and BamHI sites. Point mutations in uaf-1(stop codons), the unc-93 (e1500 mutation) or mutated transgenes were introduced using QuickChange II or III Site-Directed Mutagenesis Kit (Stratagene) with primers containing corresponding mutations. PCR was performed using Eppendorf Cyclers, and DNA products were resolved using agarose gels. DNA sequence determination was performed with an ABI Prism 3100 Genetic Analyzer. PCR primers are listed in Table S5.
###end p 116
###begin title 117
Transgene experiments
###end title 117
###begin p 118
###xml 59 63 59 63 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000708-Mello1">[82]</xref>
###xml 160 171 152 163 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Arabidopsis</italic>
###xml 392 397 372 377 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">myo-2</sub>
###xml 392 397 372 377 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><sub>myo-2</sub></italic>
###xml 160 171 <span type="species:ncbi:3702">Arabidopsis</span>
Germline transgene experiments were performed as described [82]. Transgene mixtures generally contained 20 microg/ml 1 kb DNA ladder (Invitrogen), 20 microg/ml Arabidopsis genomic DNA and 10 microg/ml of the transgene of interest. When the transgene did not cause the expression of a GFP fusion protein, 10 microg/ml pPD95.86-GFP plasmid (expressing GFP in body-wall muscles) or 5 microg/ml pmyo-2dsRED (expressing RFP in pharynx) was added to the injection mixture as a visible fluorescence marker to identify animals carrying the transgene.
###end p 118
###begin title 119
Bioinformatics
###end title 119
###begin p 120
We downloaded approximate 40,000 unique intronic sequences from WormMart (WormBase Release 195) and processed the sequences using BBEdit and MS Excel softwares. Identical 3' splice sites (positions -7 to -1) were grouped and counted.
###end p 120

uaf-1(n4588) does not reduce the mRNA levels of genes that genetically interact with unc-93. Real-time RT-PCR analyses of mRNA levels of constitutively expressed genes (act-1, gpd-2), a body wall muscle specific gene (myo-3) and genes involved in the rubberband Unc phenotype (unc-93, sup-9, sup-10, sup-18, sup-11). The levels of endogenous rpl-26 mRNA of each sample were quantified in parallel real-time RT-PCR experiments and used as loading controls. Each data set represents the average of duplicate experiments of three biological replicates of synchronized L1 animals. Error bars, standard errors.

uaf-1 RNAi reduces UAF-1 protein level. (A) Animals were fed bacteria expressing control empty vector or dsRNA targeting uaf-1. A western blot was prepared using a UAF-1 polyclonal antibody [45] and total protein extracted from these RNAi-treated animals. uaf-1(RNAi) dramatically reduced the protein level of UAF-1. (B) Coomassie blue staining indicated that the loading of total protein was similar among the samples. (C) Quantification using NIH ImageJ software of UAF-1 levels in wild-type or unc-93(e1500) animals treated with either control empty vector or uaf-1(RNAi). uaf-1(RNAi) treatment reduced UAF-1 levels in both wild-type and unc-93(e1500) animals (35% and 23% of the levels in animals treated with control empty vectors, respectively).
