###xml 429 441 429 441 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
###xml 472 478 472 478 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 540 546 540 546 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 623 629 623 629 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 672 684 672 684 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
###xml 686 698 686 698 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 703 715 703 715 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 717 729 717 729 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10(n983)</italic>
uaf-1(n4588) and sfa-1(n4562) do not cause obvious alternative splicing of the sup-10 transcript. (A) Total RNAs from animals of the indicated genotypes were prepared and RT-PCR experiments were performed to amplify the full-length sup-10 cDNA using PCR primers covering the 5' start codon and the 3' stop codon. No sup-10 transcript with an abnormal size was detected for wild-type, sup-10(n983), uaf-1(n4588) and uaf-1(n4588); sup-10(n983) animals. DNA sequences of the sup-10 RT-PCR bands from all the four genotypes were determined. No sup-10 transcript with altered splicing was observed. (B) No alternatively spliced sup-10 transcript was identified from wild-type, sup-10(n983), sfa-1(n4562) and sfa-1(n4562); sup-10(n983) animals using RT-PCR experiments and DNA sequence determination. Genotypes are indicated at the top.

###xml 17 29 17 29 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 156 168 156 168 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 173 185 173 185 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 297 309 297 309 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 311 323 311 323 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 504 516 504 516 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 518 530 518 530 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sfa-1(n4562)</italic>
###xml 664 686 <span type="species:ncbi:6239">Caenorhabditis elegans</span>
uaf-1(n4588) and sfa-1(n4562) cause synthetic lethality. Anesthesized animals of the indicated genotypes were observed with Nomarski optics. For wild-type, uaf-1(n4588) and sfa-1(n4562), animals were photographed 24 hours after the mid-L4 stage (based on vulval invagination [Herman, et al]). For uaf-1(n4588); sfa-1(n4562) double mutants, animals were observed each day for up to ten days after hatching. No animals grew beyond the size of a wild-type animal of the L2 larval stage. Two escapers of the uaf-1(n4588); sfa-1(n4562) genotype that survived embryonic lethality are shown. Scale bar: 200 microm. (Herman T, Hartwieg E, Horvitz HR (1999) sqv mutants of Caenorhabditis elegans are defective in vulval epithelial invagination. Proc Natl Acad Sci U S A 96: 968-973.)

###begin p 134
###xml 0 12 0 12 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 81 87 81 87 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 89 94 89 94 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 99 105 99 105 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 166 171 166 171 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1</italic>
###xml 199 205 199 205 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 207 222 207 222 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9 or sup-10</italic>
###xml 262 274 262 274 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 295 301 295 301 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 303 308 303 308 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9</italic>
###xml 312 318 312 318 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-10</italic>
###xml 322 334 322 334 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 446 458 446 458 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 479 485 479 485 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-58</italic>
###xml 487 493 487 493 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">egl-23</italic>
###xml 498 504 498 504 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">twk-18</italic>
###xml 655 667 655 667 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">uaf-1(n4588)</italic>
###xml 672 684 672 684 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e444)</italic>
###xml 688 700 688 700 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e669)</italic>
###xml 753 765 753 765 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e444)</italic>
###xml 769 781 769 781 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-52(e669)</italic>
uaf-1(n4588) does not cause synthetic defects with loss-of-function mutations of unc-93, sup-9 and sup-10 and does not suppress other Unc mutants. To examine whether uaf-1 functions redundantly with unc-93, sup-9 or sup-10, we compared double mutants containing uaf-1(n4588) and lf mutations of unc-93, sup-9 or sup-10 to uaf-1(n4588) single mutants for locomotion, growth, and gross morphology. No differences were observed. Double mutants with uaf-1(n4588) and gf mutations of unc-58, egl-23 and twk-18 were compared to single mutants carrying these gf mutations, and no visible suppression of the Unc phenotypes was observed. Double mutants containing uaf-1(n4588) and unc-52(e444) or unc-52(e669) mutations were compared to single mutants of either unc-52(e444) or unc-52(e669) mutations, and no visible suppression of the Unc phenotypes was observed. Pvl: protruding vulva. Ste: sterile. Dpy: dumpy. Egl: egg-laying defective.

###begin p 137
###xml 26 32 26 32 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 160 166 160 166 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 173 179 173 179 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 227 239 223 235 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">sup-9(n1550)</italic>
###xml 247 258 243 254 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(lr12</italic>
###xml 315 321 307 313 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
The alternatively spliced unc-93 transcript does not encode a functional UNC-93 protein product. Transgenes driving the expression of the alternatively spliced unc-93 cDNA (unc-93 cDNA(Delta)) did not rescue the suppression of sup-9(n1550) by the unc-93(lr12Delta) mutation, while transgenes expressing a wild-type unc-93 cDNA rescued the suppression.
###end p 137

###begin p 140
###xml 26 32 26 32 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 151 157 151 157 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 219 232 215 228 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 282 288 278 284 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 347 353 343 349 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 426 439 422 435 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93(e1500)</italic>
###xml 447 453 443 449 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 502 508 494 500 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 532 538 524 530 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
###xml 567 573 555 561 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">unc-93</italic>
The alternatively spliced unc-93 transcript likely does not encode a dominant-negative UNC-93 protein product. Tansgenes driving the expression of the unc-93 cDNA(Delta) did not suppress the rubberband Unc phenotype of unc-93(e1500) animals, while transgenes expressing a wild type unc-93 cDNA suppressed the Unc phenotype. As loss of function of unc-93 results in phenotypically wild-type animals, the lack of suppression of unc-93(e1500) by the unc-93(Delta) transgenes suggests that the function of unc-93 was not antagonized by unc-93(Delta), indicating that the unc-93(Delta) cDNA does not encode a dominant-negative UNC-93 protein.
###end p 140

Sequences and distributions of the three 3' splice sites we analyzed. Approximate 40,000 unique introns were analyzed, and the numbers and ratios of all types of 3' splice sites were calculated.
